<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>But why's she got to go to the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Library" title="Hogwarts Library">library</a>?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ronald Weasley</b>: "<i>Because that's what Hermione does. When in doubt, go to the library.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione's dependency on books<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p><b>Minister Hermione Jean</b><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><b> Granger</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/19_September" title="19 September">19 September</a>, <a href="/wiki/1979" title="1979">1979</a><sup id="cite_ref-birthday_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthday-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>) was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a><sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a> born to <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_father" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s father">Mr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_mother" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s mother">Mrs Granger</a>. At the age of eleven, she learned about her <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> nature and was accepted into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Hermione began attending Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> and was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>. She possessed a brilliant academic mind and proved to be a gifted student in almost every subject that she studied. 
</p><p>Hermione first met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> aboard the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, who found her unfriendly and somewhat of an "insufferable know-it-all",  an impression reinforced by her constant correct answers and eagerness to please the <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professors</a>. However, she stepped in to take the blame from the boys after they had saved her from a <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">troll</a> on <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en" title="Hallowe&#39;en">Hallowe'en</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, surprising them in a grateful way, which led to them quickly becoming friends. She later played a crucial role in protecting the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> from <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>.   
</p><p>In her second year, Hermione had a key role in the discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, before falling victim to the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s basilisk">basilisk</a> unleashed upon Hogwarts following the opening of the Chamber. However, she recovered from the <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrification</a> under the care of <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> with <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a>. The next year, Hermione was granted permission to use a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> from the Ministry of Magic to facilitate her volition to study far more subjects than were possible without time travel, though she and Harry later used it to rescue <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> the <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a> from execution.   
</p><p>During her fourth year, Hermione became an advocate for the better treatment of <a href="/wiki/House-elves" class="mw-redirect" title="House-elves">house-elves</a>, forming the association <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">S.P.E.W.</a>, and helped in Harry's preparation for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. In her fifth year, Hermione was the driving force behind the creation of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> and fought alongside fellow D.A. members in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. In her sixth year, Hermione continued her role as <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a> and fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>.   
</p><p>Hermione played a significant role in many other battles of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, as well. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, she fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, alongside the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Hermione and Ron decided not to return to Hogwarts for their final year of studies, instead choosing to accompany Harry on his quest to find and destroy Lord Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux-making_spell" title="Horcrux-making spell">Horcruxes</a>, a quest in which several of her actions were essential. She destroyed <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" title="Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Hufflepuff's Cup</a>, a Horcrux, with Ron using a basilisk fang found in the Chamber of Secrets. Hermione then fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, helping in the defeat of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> who tortured her: <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>.  
</p><p>Following the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Hermione went back to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> to complete her education. She later found employment with the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, furthering the cause for the better treatment of house-elves. Afterward, she was promoted to the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a>, where she dedicated herself to eradicating old laws that were biased in favour of <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-bloods</a>. Hermione eventually married Ron Weasley and together they had two children, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a>. She became the godmother of Harry and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> Potter's eldest son <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James</a>. By the year <a href="/wiki/2019" title="2019">2019</a>, Hermione had become the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1979-1991)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281979-1991.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1979-1991)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1979-1991)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1979-1991)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/47/Granger_family_DH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160712202711" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="143" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Granger family DH.jpg" data-image-key="Granger_family_DH.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/47/Granger_family_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20160712202711" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/47/Granger_family_DH.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160712202711" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/47/Granger_family_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20160712202711" decoding="async" width="240" height="143" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Granger family DH.jpg" data-image-key="Granger_family_DH.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/47/Granger_family_DH.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20160712202711" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Granger_family_DH.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A young Hermione with her parents</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was born to <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_father" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s father">Mr</a>. and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_mother" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s mother">Mrs Granger</a> on <a href="/wiki/19_September" title="19 September">19 September</a> <a href="/wiki/1979" title="1979">1979</a>. She was their only child<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and, although they were "a bit bemused" by the oddities displayed by their daughter, they were known to be proud of her.
</p><p>Upon turning eleven, Hermione was happily surprised to learn that she was a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a> and was therefore invited to attend <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She eagerly accepted and took to studying magic even before she began her first year at Hogwarts in the <a href="/wiki/September" title="September">September</a> of 1991, learning all the set spellbooks by heart and even managing to <a href="/wiki/Underage_magic" title="Underage magic">perform</a> "a few spells" successfully. In addition to the texts set by the school, Hermione brought with her several other books for reference and to further her understanding of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> to the point that she had looked at books and had more knowledge of the wizarding world than some of her <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a>/<a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> classmates.
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1991-1997)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281991-1997.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1991-1997)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1997)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1997)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Terry Boot</b>: "<i>How come you're not in Ravenclaw? With brains like yours?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Well, the Sorting Hat did seriously consider putting me in Ravenclaw during my Sorting, but it decided on Gryffindor in the end.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione's use of the advanced <a href="/wiki/Protean_Charm" title="Protean Charm">Protean Charm</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>Hermione enjoyed her years as a pupil at Hogwarts and took assignments, classes, and school rules very seriously. She was often described as brilliant, to the point of being said to be "<i>the brightest witch of her age</i>". Her favourite subject was initially <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a>, and later <a href="/wiki/Arithmancy" title="Arithmancy">Arithmancy</a>. Given her keen mind, some students - such as <a href="/wiki/Terry_Boot" title="Terry Boot">Terry Boot</a> - wondered why Hermione was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> rather than <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>. She admitted that the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> did consider putting her in Ravenclaw.
</p><p>It is likely that the Sorting Hat ultimately put her in Gryffindor after stalling for about 4 minutes, because Hermione chose to be in it, just like Harry chose to not be in Slytherin. On the train she states that, "<i>Gryffindor... sounds by far the best.</i>" She proved her rightful place in Gryffindor with her steadfast bravery and loyalty to her friends, <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. After being Sorted into Gryffindor, Hermione shared a dormitory with <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati Patil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fay_Dunbar" title="Fay Dunbar">Fay Dunbar</a> and a ginger girl.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In spite of always wanting to follow the school rules, after Hermione became friends with Harry and Ron, she would disobey the rules along with them in order to successfully complete their group affairs. For example, she went with Ron and Harry into the third-floor corridor in their first year, which students were temporarily forbidden from entering, in order to save the Philosopher's Stone; she assisted in creating the Polyjuice Potion in their second year; and although Harry was the one who taught Dumbledore's Army in their fifth year, she was the one who came up with the idea.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_year">First year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Harry_and_Ron">Meeting Harry and Ron</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry and Ron">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry and Ron"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Has anyone seen a toad? Neville's lost one</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione's first interaction with Harry Potter and Ron Weasley<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160215161419" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio meet.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_meet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160215161419" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio meet.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_meet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_meet.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio meet for the first time aboard the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was a couple of weeks away from turning twelve when she boarded the Hogwarts Express in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, where she met Harry Potter and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> while helping <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> find his pet <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>. Hermione demonstrated knowledge and talent with <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> beyond most of those her age, despite having only recently discovered that she was a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>. She wished to be a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>, and her wish was granted considering she did get sorted into Gryffindor.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407141259" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="178" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PS Wingardium Leviosa feather.gif" data-image-key="PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/178?cb=20140407141259" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140407141259" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/178?cb=20140407141259" decoding="async" width="178" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PS Wingardium Leviosa feather.gif" data-image-key="PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a1/PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/178?cb=20140407141259" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PS_Wingardium_Leviosa_feather.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione Granger casting a spell perfectly, also correcting <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, showing her knowledge of spells</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150718235057" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150718235057" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150718235057" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150718235057" decoding="async" width="180" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/40/Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150718235057" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-sorting1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione being <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">sorted</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione soon proved to be the best in all her classes, eager to please the professors and to help others learn, albeit in a bossy way that made it difficult for her to make friends. Although she was a know-it-all, Hermione did often help Neville Longbottom, who struggled in most classes other than <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Hermione strictly followed all school rules and tried to prevent other students from breaking rules and getting into trouble. On one night, she followed Harry and Ron as they were leaving Gryffindor Tower to <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duel</a> <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. They were chased by <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, acting on a tipoff by Malfoy, into the third-floor corridor — forbidden to students — where they came face-to-face with <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, a three-headed dog belonging to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>. Later on, she argued that her spying was to their benefit when she pointed out the dog had been standing on a trapdoor, which neither Harry nor Ron had noticed.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span id="Hallowe'en"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hallowe.27en">Hallowe'en</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hallowe&#039;en">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Hallowe&#039;en"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/First_floor_girls_bathroom.png/revision/latest?cb=20131021031612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="First floor girls bathroom.png" data-image-key="First_floor_girls_bathroom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/First_floor_girls_bathroom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131021031612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/First_floor_girls_bathroom.png/revision/latest?cb=20131021031612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/First_floor_girls_bathroom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131021031612" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="First floor girls bathroom.png" data-image-key="First_floor_girls_bathroom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/First_floor_girls_bathroom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131021031612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:First_floor_girls_bathroom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The mountain troll entering the bathroom that Hermione's in during the Hallowe'en feast</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>There are some things you can't share without ending up liking each other, and knocking out a twelve-foot mountain troll is one of them</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;The creation of the trio's special friendship<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>The friendship between Harry, Ron and Hermione was solidified when, on <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">Hallowe'en</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, the three were forced to confront <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell%27s_first_mountain_troll" title="Quirinus Quirrell&#39;s first mountain troll">a mountain troll</a>, which had been secretly let into the school by Professor <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>. Unaware that a troll was on the loose in the school, Hermione had spent that day crying in the girls' bathroom after overhearing Ron making unkind comments about her. The troll made its way into the bathroom she was in, and Harry and Ron came to her rescue, saving her. When Professors <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> arrived at the scene, Hermione covered for the boys, claiming she was fighting the troll because she had thought that she could manage, having read a great deal about them and that Ron and Harry had merely come to help her escape. From then on, the three students were best friends and spent large amounts of time together.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span id="Hagrid's_dragon"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hagrid.27s_dragon">Hagrid's dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s dragon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Hagrid&#039;s dragon"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/56/Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170809231614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione sets fire to cloak.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/56/Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170809231614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/56/Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170809231614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/56/Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170809231614" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione sets fire to cloak.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/56/Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170809231614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_sets_fire_to_cloak.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione setting Snape's robes on fire during a Quidditch match</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The incident with the troll was by no means her only adventure in that first year. During the first <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match, Hermione set <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>'s robes on <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">fire</a> when she thought he was <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxing</a> Harry's broom. In the spring of <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>, now a friend of Hermione's through Harry, managed to procure a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_egg" title="Dragon egg">Dragon egg</a>, the unlicensed possession of which was illegal. The three children secretly helped Hagrid care for the beast, which he'd named <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a>. When the dragon was discovered, she and Harry smuggled it out of the school to some friends of Ron's elder brother, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie Weasley</a>, who worked as a dragon-tamer. On their way back to the dormitories they were caught by <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, who escorted them to Professor Minerva McGonagall. Along with Neville and Draco, they received detention and had 50 points deducted each from their respective houses.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>After their run-in with Fluffy, Harry deduced that whatever Hagrid had retrieved from <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> was beneath the trapdoor. Hagrid let it slip that <i>"... What's under that trapdoor is strictly between <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicholas Flamel</a>"</i>. After much research turned up nothing, Harry was given a Dumbledore <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Card</a> by Neville, which mentions Dumbledore's work in <a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a> with Flamel. This led Hermione to look at a large book on Alchemy which she had borrowed from the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Library" title="Hogwarts Library">library</a> for "<i>a bit of light reading</i>". After consulting the book, she realised that Fluffy was guarding the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Underground_Chambers">The Underground Chambers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Underground Chambers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: The Underground Chambers"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/BluebellFlames.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090725161636" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="BluebellFlames.jpg" data-image-key="BluebellFlames.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/BluebellFlames.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090725161636" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/BluebellFlames.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090725161636" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/BluebellFlames.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090725161636" decoding="async" width="180" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="BluebellFlames.jpg" data-image-key="BluebellFlames.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/BluebellFlames.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20090725161636" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:BluebellFlames.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione conjuring the Bluebell flames</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706032727" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-trio chess.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706032727" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706032727" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706032727" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-trio chess.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d7/Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706032727" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-trio_chess.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio stand as a unified front during the human chess match</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Fearing that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> would return if he stole the stone, and believing that Snape was acting as a double agent and attempting to steal it, Harry decided to steal it first. When he told Hermione that he could go on alone, she rebuffed him. After the trio passed <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>, it was Hermione who freed Ron from a patch of <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a> he had dropped into by conjuring <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">Bluebell Flames</a>. She later got herself and Harry through a challenge involving a <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Potion Riddle</a> in order to obtain the right potion between many of them. Hermione used her logic to figure out the riddle and let Harry go forward without her, as there was only enough potion for one person.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>
Later, at the Farewell Feast in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, Hermione, Harry, Ron, and Neville were all awarded extra House Points for bravery and heroism, allowing <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> to win the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Hermione earned her 10 points by correctly solving Professor Snape’s potion riddle.</p><div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span>"<i> Second -- to Miss Hermione Granger... for the use of cool logic in the face of fire, I award Gryffindor house fifty points.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, giving points to Hermione Granger during the end-of-term feast of 1991</dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_year">Second year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Second year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Well, if you two are going to chicken out, fine. I don't want to break rules, you know. I think threatening <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> is far worse than brewing up a difficult potion. But if you don't want to find out....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>I never thought I'd see the day when you'd be persuading us to break rules.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione breaking school rules in an attempt to catch the Heir of Slytherin<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Before she started her second year, Hermione wrote several letters to Harry at <a href="/wiki/Privet_Drive" title="Privet Drive">Privet Drive</a>, all of which were intercepted by <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>, as the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a> wanted Harry to believe that his friends had forgotten him in order to prevent his return to Hogwarts. She and <a href="/wiki/Granger_family" title="Granger family">her parents</a> also accompanied Harry and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> to shop for school supplies.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170601155453" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2 draco hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170601155453" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170601155453" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170601155453" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2 draco hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170601155453" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2_draco_hermione.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Draco Malfoy calling Hermione the derogatory slur "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It was during her second school year that Hermione first encountered the prejudice and hatred surrounding her <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood status</a>, when <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> called her a "<i>filthy little Mudblood</i>" after she told him off for insulting the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>. Hermione had never heard the highly offensive term but looking around at everyone around her, it was an obvious fact. <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> lunged at him, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> even tried to hex him, but it backfired, as his wand had been damaged. To help Hermione feel better about the incident, Hagrid urged her not to think about it, pointing out that she was a talented witch, regardless of what bigoted people said about her <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> status.
</p><p>Harry and Ron were surprised, and Ron annoyed, by Hermione's obvious crush on <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, who became that year's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor. She scored full marks on the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_Second_Year_Essential_Knowledge_Test" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts Second Year Essential Knowledge Test">first quiz in his class</a>, which consisted entirely of questions pertaining to Lockhart's books, including a question regarding his favourite colour (lilac) that most of the class had answered incorrectly. In fact, she went as far as to doodle hearts on her DADA assignments, not knowing until later that he was, in reality, a self-obsessed fraud.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170831193739" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio writing on wall.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170831193739" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio writing on wall.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The writing on the wall and the petrified form of <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en" title="Hallowe&#39;en">Hallowe'en</a>, <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a> Hermione attended <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington%27s_five-hundredth_Deathday_Party" title="Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington&#39;s five-hundredth Deathday Party">Nearly Headless Nick's Deathday Party</a> with Harry and Ron. Whilst heading back upstairs, she followed Harry in a detour, after he claimed to be hearing voices. They discovered the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Caretaker" title="Hogwarts Caretaker">caretaker</a>'s cat, <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a>, petrified and the walls vandalised. Hermione began spending all her free time in the Hogwarts Library after she saw the writing on the corridor walls, which had said that the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> had been re-opened. Despite hoping to read about the legend, she could not, as all the books had been previously checked out.
</p><p>Hermione shocked everyone when she actually interrupted <a href="/wiki/Cuthbert_Binns" title="Cuthbert Binns">Professor Binns</a> during a <a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a> class, asking about the Chamber of Secrets. This was the only known time when a student had asked the boring professor a question, and the class was interested in what he had to say. Professor Binns had stated that <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a> had hidden a chamber which consisted of a horrible monster. It had been unleashed before once by an "<a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Heir of Slytherin</a>", petrifying many Muggle-born and had also killed a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> girl, named <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Myrtle Warren</a>, who began haunting the girls' lavatory and became known as Moaning Myrtle. Slytherin, a pure-blood loyalist, was against Muggle-born children being allowed to attend Hogwarts, but he was outnumbered by the other founders and Muggle-borns like Hermione were permitted as students. Slytherin fled the school, but rumours spread that he had built a hidden chamber; it was said that the school had been searched many times, but no such chamber had been found.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/Brewing_potions.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720160320" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brewing potions.jpg" data-image-key="Brewing_potions.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/Brewing_potions.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720160320" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/Brewing_potions.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720160320" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/Brewing_potions.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720160320" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brewing potions.jpg" data-image-key="Brewing_potions.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/Brewing_potions.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720160320" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Brewing_potions.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione brewing <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>, used by the trio in an attempt to gain information from Draco Malfoy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry proposed the theory that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> was the Heir of Slytherin, Hermione and Ron agreed. Hermione suggested that they brew <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice</a> Potion, and temporarily transform themselves into Slytherin students in an attempt to find out the truth. She went even further by daring to check <i><a href="/wiki/Moste_Potente_Potions" title="Moste Potente Potions">Moste Potente Potions</a></i> out of the library using a note from Professor Lockhart - who had no idea what the book was - in the desire to research the potion. The book was in the <a href="/wiki/Restricted_Section" title="Restricted Section">Restricted Section</a> and therefore unavailable to younger students without permission from a teacher. She hoped that they would be able to obtain a viable confession from Malfoy, if he was unaware he was being interrogated. She brewed the potion in Moaning Myrtle's bathroom, as no one used it due to Myrtle herself being highly irritating. She also risked serious consequences when she stole potion ingredients from <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_storeroom" class="mw-redirect" title="Severus Snape&#39;s storeroom">personal cupboards</a> that were needed for the difficult potion, which took a month to brew.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cf/Harry-Potter-and-the-Chamber-of-Secrets-2002-books-male-characters-29996396-500-375.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170925195204" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" class="image"><img alt="" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-Potter-and-the-Chamber-of-Secrets-2002-books-male-characters-29996396-500-375.jpg" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-Potter-and-the-Chamber-of-Secrets-2002-books-male-characters-29996396-500-375.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio discuss possible theories behind Tom Riddle's mysterious diary</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unfortunately, Hermione was unable to join Harry and Ron in the ruse with Polyjuice Potion because the hair she obtained from Slytherin <a href="/wiki/Millicent_Bulstrode" title="Millicent Bulstrode">Millicent Bulstrode</a> during their scuffle in the <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a> was actually the hair of Bulstrode's cat. Hermione grew fur and a tail and remained in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> for weeks as she did not transform back when the normal duration of effectiveness - one hour - was up. Harry and Ron, however, were able to use the potion she brewed to transform into <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>, respectively. They entered the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Dungeon" title="Slytherin Dungeon">common room</a>, and through conversation with <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, realised that he was not the Heir of Slytherin, and was not involved in the opening of the Chamber after all.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Petrified_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190207225207" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="218" height="90" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Petrified Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Petrified_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Petrified_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/218?cb=20190207225207" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Petrified_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190207225207" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Petrified_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/218?cb=20190207225207" decoding="async" width="218" height="90" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Petrified Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Petrified_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Petrified_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/218?cb=20190207225207" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Petrified_Hermione.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A Petrified Hermione in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Months after her recovery from the Polyjuice complication, Hermione suffered another accident. Drawing the connection between Harry hearing voices in the walls and him being a Parselmouth, she came to the conclusion that the creature attacking students must be a <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Basilisk</a>, and rushed to the library to conduct further research. On her way back from the library, she warned the first person she saw, <a href="/wiki/Penelope_Clearwater" title="Penelope Clearwater">Penelope Clearwater</a>, and advised her to look around corners with a mirror before going anywhere. It saved both their lives, because they were both <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> when they spotted the basilisk's eyes through the mirror instead of dying immediately as they would have done if they'd looked straight into its eyes.
</p><p>Though she was petrified for the rest of the school year, Hermione was still able to assist Harry and Ron, for she had torn out the page on basilisks and scribbled on it "<i><b>pipes</b>"</i>, referencing the manner in which the creature had moved around the school undetected. Harry and Ron found it clenched in her hand when they were finally allowed to visit her in the Hospital Wing. Using this note and other information they had gathered, Harry and Ron were able to successfully put an end to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s plans to resurrect his body through his memory stored in <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">an old school diary</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Hermione_unpetrified.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170918161141" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione unpetrified.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_unpetrified.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Hermione_unpetrified.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170918161141" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Hermione_unpetrified.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170918161141" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Hermione_unpetrified.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170918161141" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione unpetrified.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_unpetrified.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Hermione_unpetrified.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170918161141" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_unpetrified.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A fully recovered Hermione</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was later cured with a <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a> created by <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a>. Upon arriving at the Great Hall, she was immediately greeted by Nearly Headless Nick. After hugging Harry she exchanged an awkward greeting with Ron. Hermione was disappointed to learn that, as a special treat for the school, Professor Dumbledore cancelled the students' end of year exams, but she was intensely proud that her friends had solved the mystery.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> That summer, Hermione went on holiday to <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> with her <a href="/wiki/Granger_family" title="Granger family">parents</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_year">Third year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Third year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Third year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>P-P-Professor McGonagall! Sh-she said I'd failed everything!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione facing her <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417014719" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="90" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C4M2 Magical Menagerie.png" data-image-key="B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417014719" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png/revision/latest?cb=20180417014719" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417014719" decoding="async" width="250" height="90" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C4M2 Magical Menagerie.png" data-image-key="B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180417014719" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C4M2_Magical_Menagerie.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione adopting Crookshanks from the <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Magical Menagerie</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Just before she began the 1993-1994 school year, while visiting <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> with Harry and the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>, Hermione met and adopted a ginger part-<a href="/wiki/Kneazle" title="Kneazle">Kneazle</a> cat named <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Magical Menagerie</a>. However, her new bond with her cat caused friction with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and his pet rat <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>, as Crookshanks was always trying to catch the rat. Also at the beginning of this school year, Hermione obtained a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> from Professor McGonagall so she could double up on classes, though this was kept secret from everyone, even Harry and Ron.
</p><p>When Harry received a <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Firebolt" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Firebolt">Firebolt</a> for Christmas with no note, Hermione reported it to Professor McGonagall, thinking it was sent by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, whom everyone believed to be a dangerous murderer who was after Harry. His broom was taken away to be inspected, which caused a temporary rift between the two friends. There was a further social strain for Hermione when Ron accused Crookshanks of eating Scabbers, who had disappeared.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170808144851" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione punching Draco GIF.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170808144851" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20170808144851" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170808144851" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione punching Draco GIF.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/35/Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170808144851" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_punching_Draco_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione hitting Draco Malfoy for cruelly mocking <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione poured herself into defending <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a> on trial before the <a href="/wiki/Committee_for_the_Disposal_of_Dangerous_Creatures" title="Committee for the Disposal of Dangerous Creatures">Committee for the Disposal of Dangerous Creatures</a> for attacking <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> during a <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> class. Once the trio reconciled, after Hagrid told Harry and Ron how disappointed he was when they selfishly put the Firebolt and Scabbers over their friendship with Hermione, they apologised. Their attempt to save Buckbeak failed, as <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> frightened the Committee into deciding that the creature would be executed. Hermione was extremely upset by this news and grew furious to the point of slapping Draco Malfoy when he dared to mock Hagrid for his tears and being upset over Buckbeak's fate.
</p><p>That year, Hermione was among the students who found <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> to be the best <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher they have ever had. She cleverly deduced that Professor Lupin was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>, based on his Boggart taking the form of a full moon, the timing of his unexplained absences from class, and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> changing a lesson he took over to the subject of werewolves even though it wasn't due on the syllabus for weeks. However, she didn't expose Lupin, presumably because she believed he was a good teacher and didn't agree with the prejudice many hold against werewolves. 
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, on the other hand, turned out to be a subject Hermione had no respect for or interest in, and soon dropped the subject after Professor <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> told her that she did not posses the <a href="/wiki/Inner_Eye" title="Inner Eye">Second Sight</a> and because she believed that Divination was an imprecise branch of magic.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Rescue_of_Sirius_Black_and_Buckbeak">Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161208053517" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="164" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Encounter in the Shrieking Shack.jpg" data-image-key="Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208053517" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161208053517" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208053517" decoding="async" width="250" height="164" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Encounter in the Shrieking Shack.jpg" data-image-key="Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161208053517" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Encounter_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professor Lupin and Sirius Black with the trio, before forcing <a href="/wiki/Pettigrew_family" title="Pettigrew family">Pettigrew</a> into human form</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the day of Buckbeak's execution, the trio ventured down to console Hagrid. While in his cabin, Hermione discovered <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>, Ron's lost rat. Hagrid urged them to leave and they witnessed from a distance what they believed to be Buckbeak's execution. Before they could return to their dormitory, Scabbers bit Ron and fled. While chasing after the rat, they were attacked by a <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">black dog</a>, which pulled Ron by the leg into a tunnel beneath the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>, which then attacked them.
</p><p>Afterward, Hermione and Harry hurried after them eventually arriving in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, where Sirius Black, whose <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form was the black dog, confronted them. They were soon joined by Professor Lupin who was acting strangely, and Hermione told Harry and Ron of her belief that he was a werewolf, which he then confirmed. It was revealed that Sirius had been framed for the betrayal of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>, and that the true traitor was Peter Pettigrew, who had been hiding from the world as Ron's pet rat. Hermione also cast <i><a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Expelliarmus</a></i> on Snape when he discovered them, knocking him out, at which she was horrified.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424032640" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="90" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C20M2 Lake surrounded by Dementors.png" data-image-key="B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424032640" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424032640" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424032640" decoding="async" width="250" height="90" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C20M2 Lake surrounded by Dementors.png" data-image-key="B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424032640" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C20M2_Lake_surrounded_by_Dementors.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry, Hermione, and Sirius being attacked by Dementors at the Black Lake</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once it had been decided that Pettigrew would be turned over to the authorities rather than murdered, the motley group left the Shrieking Shack. When the full moon appeared, chaos ensued as Lupin transformed into a werewolf as, due to the chaotic turn of events, he hadn't taken the <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane</a> potion that Professor Snape produced for him monthly in order for him to retain his humanity. In the chaos, Pettigrew attacked Ron and escaped, and Sirius had to transform into his dog form in order to protect Harry, Ron, and Hermione from the werewolf. Lupin was eventually distracted by a howl from the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>. Hermione and Harry rushed to Sirius' aid when they heard him moaning, but hundreds of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> descended on them, come to recapture Sirius. Sirius quickly fainted, and Harry told Hermione to think of something happy and attempt to cast a <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">patronus</a> as he was trying to himself, but they were both unable to cast one. As Harry conjured an incorporeal Patronus, Hermione passed out, leaving Harry to fight the Dementors alone. Harry held them off for a while but was eventually overwhelmed. The Dementors were about to perform the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Kiss</a> on Harry, Hermione, and Sirius when a mysterious figure in the distance cast a very powerful <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> to repel the Dementors. Unable to see properly in the resulting blinding light, Harry thought he glimpsed his father just before he, too, lost consciousness.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Turning_time.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140717051907" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Turning time.gif" data-image-key="Turning_time.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Turning_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140717051907" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Turning_time.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140717051907" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Turning_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140717051907" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Turning time.gif" data-image-key="Turning_time.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/79/Turning_time.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140717051907" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Turning_time.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Hermione using the Time-turner</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png/revision/latest?cb=20190125003405" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="131" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA HQ still Hermione Buckbeak Harry.png" data-image-key="POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125003405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png/revision/latest?cb=20190125003405" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125003405" decoding="async" width="180" height="131" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA HQ still Hermione Buckbeak Harry.png" data-image-key="POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190125003405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_HQ_still_Hermione_Buckbeak_Harry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Harry saving Buckbeak from execution</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry and Hermione awoke in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> after being rescued by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, who conjured stretchers for Hermione, Harry and Sirius.
