After realising that Sirius' soul was to be destroyed by the Dementor's Kiss and receiving vague, though instructive and useful, instructions from <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, Hermione used her <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to return herself and Harry to a time earlier in the evening. It was a very difficult task and Harry had to be constantly reminded by Hermione to stay concealed as being seen could cause irreparable damage to their timelines. Hermione agreed with Harry that it was difficult to watch their problems again, but she strictly said that they could do nothing about it, as bad things happened to wizards who tried to meddle with their past and future lives. 
</p><p>The two did, however, successfully use the opportunity to <a href="/wiki/Rescue_of_Sirius_Black_and_Buckbeak" title="Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak">rescue</a> Sirius and also Buckbeak, as it was hinted by Dumbledore that more than one innocent life could be spared that night.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Whilst waiting, she discussed their saviour with Harry, and when Harry realised that it was not his father he saw but himself having travelled back in time, she claimed that none but a powerful wizard could have conjured a Patronus to drive away that many Dementors. As evidenced by her assertion that time-travelling was extremely dangerous, Hermione took great personal risk to save Sirius and Buckbeak. At the end of the year Hermione returned her Time-Turner, claiming it caused too much trouble and that she would drop a few subjects instead, which was a very big surprise to everyone.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_year">Fourth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fourth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Fourth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>You know, house-elves get a very raw deal! It's slavery, that's what it is! That <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Mr Crouch</a> made her go up to the top of the stadium, and she was terrified, and he's got her bewitched so she can't even run when they start trampling tents! Why doesn't anyone do something about it?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione begins her <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">campaign</a> for the better treatment of house-elves<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420183844" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C9M1 the trio seeing the Dark Mark.png" data-image-key="B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420183844" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420183844" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420183844" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C9M1 the trio seeing the Dark Mark.png" data-image-key="B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420183844" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, Harry, and Hermione after the riot of the <a href="/wiki/1994_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="1994 Quidditch World Cup">1994 Quidditch World Cup</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before her fourth year at Hogwarts, Hermione spent much of the summer holidays at the <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">Burrow</a> with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, sharing a room with <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. With the other <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a> (excluding Molly Weasley), they attended the 1994 Quidditch World Cup in <a href="/wiki/August" title="August">August</a>. After the game, the communal campsite was set upon by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Hermione, Harry, and Ron fled into the woods and witnessed the casting of <i><a href="/wiki/Morsmordre" title="Morsmordre">Morsmordre</a></i>. Initially caught up in the chaos surrounding the effort to catch the caster, she took exception to the accusations levelled against Harry, and the many wizards' treatment of the house-elf <a href="/wiki/Winky" title="Winky">Winky</a> who had also been at the scene.
</p><p>Once at Hogwarts, it was revealed to the students that former <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> (who was, in fact, a polyjuiced <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>) was to be the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, Lupin having left at the end of the previous year due to Snape outing his werewolf status. Moody was a hands-on professor who believed in a practical approach when it came to defence. One of his earliest lessons was on the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>. Hermione and her fellow classmates witnessed the curse's effects on a spider. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423212945" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dobby PM B4C21M2 DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen Moment.jpg" data-image-key="Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423212945" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423212945" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423212945" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dobby PM B4C21M2 DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen Moment.jpg" data-image-key="Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423212945" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dobby_PM_B4C21M2_DobbyAndWinkyOtherHouseElvesInHogwartsKitchen_Moment.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio visiting the house-elves in the Hogwarts kitchen</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione began a crusade for the liberation of <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a> by beginning the <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare</a>, or what she and the group called S.P.E.W, (or, as <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a> called it, "spew") having been appalled by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Bartemius Crouch</a>'s abusive treatment of his house-elf <a href="/wiki/Winky" title="Winky">Winky</a>. This did not earn her any popularity, as most believed that house-elves enjoy their work; indeed, even the house-elves did not like her campaigning. Harry, Ron, and Neville only reluctantly joined S.P.E.W., mostly in order to prevent Hermione from nagging them about it. Hagrid as well as <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> refused to join on the grounds that it would upset the house-elves. Despite this, Fred did tell Hermione how to get into the Hogwarts kitchens. One morning she (along with Harry and Ron) visited the kitchens, where she spoke to <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> and Winky. Dobby was pleased to see Harry and his friends and proceeded to tell them his struggles as a freed elf.
</p><p>While the trio were within the kitchen it was revealed that Winky was so saddened by the lose of her previous job that she had taken to drinking <a href="/wiki/Butterbeer" title="Butterbeer">Butterbeer</a>, as a means to get drunk and numb her pain. Hermione considered Dobby to be a good example of a free elf and tried to comfort Winky about being sacked by Crouch. This did little good, however, as Winky soon became upset by Hermione's claims that house-elves deserved to have holidays and wages. Winky was not the only elf bothered by this, as the other elves stated that proper house-elves would never need such things and to want them is considered very shameful.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706031156" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry &amp; Hermione talking.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_&amp;_Hermione_talking.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706031156" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170706031156" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706031156" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry &amp; Hermione talking.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_&amp;_Hermione_talking.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/27/Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170706031156" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_%26_Hermione_talking.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione believed Harry without question when he said he did not enter his name in the Triwizard Tournament</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the events surrounding Harry's name coming out of the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>, Hermione was the only student who believed Harry's innocence. In fact, she "<i>accepted his story without question</i>." Even Ron was suspicious that Harry had cheated in order to gain more glory, creating a rift between the two for some time. Hermione helped Harry prepare for the first task of the Triwizard Tournament by helping him learn useful spells. Some of the spells were <i><a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stupefy</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impedimenta</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">Accio,</a> </i>and the <a href="/wiki/Four-Point_Spell" title="Four-Point Spell">Four-Point Spell</a><i>. </i>She also tried to get Harry and Ron to talk to one another multiple times.
</p><p>Hermione unknowingly attracted the interest of <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang</a> Triwizard Champion and Bulgarian International <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>, <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>. He was attracted to her due to her intelligence, unconventional beauty, and the manner in which she declined to hound him for autographs, unlike other girls. Krum began following Hermione to the library and other places around Hogwarts, including the library. This was something that Hermione found very irritating, as she couldn't work when surrounded by giggling girls, who had taken it upon themselves to follow Krum throughout the castle and the school grounds. Krum even bizarrely asked Harry if it was all right for him to pursue Hermione. He eventually asked her to attend the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with him, and she accepted, not telling anyone but <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> that she was his date.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 207px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/Yule_ball7.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818144828" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="205" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Yule ball7.gif" data-image-key="Yule_ball7.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/Yule_ball7.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/205?cb=20140818144828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/Yule_ball7.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818144828" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/Yule_ball7.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/205?cb=20140818144828" decoding="async" width="205" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Yule ball7.gif" data-image-key="Yule_ball7.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b3/Yule_ball7.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/205?cb=20140818144828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Yule_ball7.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione dancing with her date, Viktor Krum at the Yule Ball</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thus, when the pair arrived, many were stunned and jealous. Hermione wore robes of a "<i>floaty, periwinkle-blue material,</i>" and her hair in an "<i>elegant knot at the back of her head</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> The attention to her appearance was unusual, and she received many positive remarks on it. Even Draco Malfoy and <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> had nothing negative to say. Hermione commented that she had used <a href="/wiki/Sleekeazy%27s_Hair_Potion" title="Sleekeazy&#39;s Hair Potion">Sleekeazy's Hair Potion</a>, but that it was too much work to use it every day. Upon seeing Hermione with Krum, Ron was overcome with jealousy. Hermione had hoped for Ron to ask her, but his invitation was insensitive and at the last minute due to him not being able to find anyone else. The two rowed about it in the common room after the ball, in which she revealed that he should have asked her properly and not <i>"as a last resort"</i>, but Ron misunderstood the point. After that, the two were seemingly more polite to each other, although more distant for a time and Ron continued to show dislike and distrust towards Krum.
</p><p>Hermione was chosen as a "kidnap victim" for Krum during the Tournament's Second Task, something that she subsequently endured teasing over. She was taken to the bottom of the Black Lake to await rescue from Krum, who donned a half-shark <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>. Krum managed to rescue her and carried her to the surface, where he revealed to her later that he "<i>never felt this way about any other girl</i>" and asked her to visit him in <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a> over the summer.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Krum was jealous of Hermione's relationship with Harry Potter, thinking that there was something romantic between them that went beyond just plain friendship. The jealousy was founded based on the lies in the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a> and </i>Harry was quick to inform Krum of these lies.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180424053809" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C28M1 Hermione opening hate mails.jpg" data-image-key="B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424053809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180424053809" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424053809" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C28M1 Hermione opening hate mails.jpg" data-image-key="B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f6/B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424053809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C28M1_Hermione_opening_hate_mails.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione receives hate mail from the readers of <i><a href="/wiki/Witch_Weekly" title="Witch Weekly">Witch Weekly</a></i> in response to Skeeter's article</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, a journalist for the <i>Daily Prophet</i> and unregistered <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>, was hiding in beetle form in Hermione's hair during this conversation. Hermione had previously reprimanded Skeeter for printing horrible lies about Harry and <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>. This angered the journalist, who wrote a scathing article on "the devious Miss Granger", claiming that she was toying with both Harry and Krum's affections and that she had developed a taste for famous wizards. Skeeter even went so far to claim that Hermione was possibly brewing <a href="/wiki/Love_Potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Love Potion">love potions</a>. In the words of Ron, Skeeter was making Hermione out to be a "<i>Scarlet Woman</i>", a phrase which made Hermione laugh. She called Hermione "<i>plain</i>" in the article, in spite of previously reporting Hermione as Harry's "<i>stunningly pretty... girlfriend</i>" by likely twisting and sensationalising the words of <a href="/wiki/Colin_Creevey" title="Colin Creevey">Colin Creevey</a> and thus using this as the basis for the article. Although Hermione found the lies ridiculous, some people believed them and started sending Hermione hate mail, including one filled with <a href="/wiki/Bubotuber_Pus" class="mw-redirect" title="Bubotuber Pus">Bubotuber Pus</a>, and even <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> treated her coldly until Harry corrected her. Hermione vowed to get revenge on Skeeter for her libel, and wondered how she was getting her information, as several things Skeeter knew had only been discussed in private conversations. This led her to come to the realisation that Skeeter was an illegal unregistered <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>, who took the form of a beetle to secretly witness confidential exchanges.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione was present when the Minister for Magic visited Harry in the hospital wing</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The students were shocked when Harry returned at the end of the third and final task with Cedric Diggory's dead body. Hermione was relieved to see Harry when he was brought to the infirmary by Professor Dumbledore. She was upset with <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> when he refused to believe Harry and Dumbledore about the truth of Voldemort's return. During her time with Harry in the Hospital Wing, she noticed Skeeter on a windowsill, attempting to eavesdrop, and captured her in the process. Hermione did not go against Harry's story when she finally heard it, sticking by her best friend.
</p><p>On the ride home on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, Hermione happily revealed to Harry and Ron that she uncovered Skeeter's status as an unregistered Animagus and had trapped her in a jar. She kept Skeeter from writing for a year by threatening to expose her to the authorities. She single-handed drove Skeeter into poverty, gaining revenge for the pain caused to Harry and her other friends. However, with the <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">return</a> of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and the murder of <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a> at the end of the school year,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> there were much more serious challenges ahead for Hermione and her friends.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_year">Fifth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fifth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Fifth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Been having a nice little chat with her about whether or not I'm a lying, attention-seeking prat, have you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>No, I told her to keep her big fat mouth shut about you, actually. And it would be quite nice if you stopped jumping down Ron and my throats, Harry, because if you haven't noticed, we're on your side.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Argument over people's differing opinions<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180420213240" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B5C6M1 Doxycide Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180420213240" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B5C6M1 Doxycide Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione with others in 12 Grimmauld Place preparing to clean</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the death of <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> refused to accept Harry and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s claims that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> had returned, and the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> labelled them either liars or nutters. However, Hermione and Ron believed Harry and defended him against the criticism of doubtful classmates. Though occasionally Harry vented his frustration at them, the two stuck by him. The trio also wanted to become members of the reconvened <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> but were not allowed to because they were under-age. Hermione helped exterminate <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>, which served as headquarters for the Order, and was immensely relieved when Harry was acquitted of the charge of having used underage magic in the presence of a muggle, after him and <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a> were attacked by a Dementor in <a href="/wiki/Little_Whinging" title="Little Whinging">Little Whinging</a>.
</p><p>Before returning to Hogwarts, she and Ron learned that they had been appointed prefects for <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house, to the secret consternation of Harry, who couldn't believe Ron had been chosen over him. She took her position very seriously. Once the school year began, Hermione resumed some of her activism on behalf of house-elves, though she was not as intense about <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">S.P.E.W.</a> as she had been the previous year. She learned how to knit socks and hats for the house-elves and hid them in Gryffindor Tower, disguising them with crumpled rubbish in an attempt to trick the house-elves into accidentally freeing themselves. The elves found this attempt insulting, and they stopped cleaning the Tower at all. <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> was the only one who enjoyed the gifts, took everything Hermione had made, and cleaned the Tower by himself, a fact which Hermione didn't know. Hermione was challenged in more ways than one that year when she met <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, whose belief in many things without logical grounds baffled Hermione. However, the two became friends after accepting one another's differences.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140609152402" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army learning Expelliarmus.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140609152402" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140609152402" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140609152402" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army learning Expelliarmus.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/88/Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140609152402" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army_learning_Expelliarmus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione practising with Dumbledore's Army in the Room of Requirement</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Meanwhile, it was not long before Hermione realised that the Ministry of Magic had decided to interfere at Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, a cruel, falsely sweet Ministry employee with a personality like "<i>poisoned honey</i>", was appointed as the new professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. She refused to teach students practical defence, focusing only on theory, despite their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">OWLs</a> being later that year. With this being the case, Hermione decided that Hogwarts needed a competent teacher and, together with Harry and Ron, founded <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, a secret organisation in which students would gather after classes and be taught practical defensive spells. She suggested that Harry be the teacher; though he originally thought the idea ridiculous, he consented to teach the class. The name was suggested by Ginny, who recalled the conversation they'd had about Fudge's greatest fear being that Dumbledore would form an army of students if the Ministry did not intervene at Hogwarts.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20100426055915" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="76" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s Patronus.gif" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_Patronus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100426055915" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20100426055915" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100426055915" decoding="async" width="180" height="76" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s Patronus.gif" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_Patronus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100426055915" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione%27s_Patronus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione conjuring her Otter Patronus</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One of the many spells Hermione learned was the <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>; hers took the corporeal form of an <a href="/wiki/Otter" title="Otter">otter</a>. Hermione became one of the few people brave enough to call <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> by his actual name. However, Hermione made the mistake of arranging the first meeting to take place in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>, as opposed to the Three Broomsticks, which Sirius, appearing in the Gryffindor Common Room fire, said would have made it a lot more harder for anyone to overhear. <a href="/wiki/Willy_Widdershins" title="Willy Widdershins">Willy Widdershins</a>, who was in the Hog's Head, went to Umbridge, who instituted <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Four" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four</a> to forbid any type of students groups from being formed under her watchful eye.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201109221209" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="StMungos PM B5C23M1 ChristmasAtStMungos Moment.jpg" data-image-key="StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201109221209" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="StMungos PM B5C23M1 ChristmasAtStMungos Moment.jpg" data-image-key="StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio and Ginny in St Mungo's after visiting Arthur Weasley</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Halfway through the year at Hogwarts, Harry had a vision of Voldemort's snake, <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, biting Mr Weasley during his task for the Order of the Phoenix. Mr Weasley was carried into <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital</a>, where Mrs Weasley screamed at him for trying to stitch his wound instead of healing it with magic. Hermione was one of the few who visited him and stayed at Number Twelve, Grimmauld Place for a couple of weeks until Mr Weasley was nursed back to health. Hermione had managed to convince her parents by telling them that skiing wasn't <i>really</i> her thing and that people who were serious about their exams stayed at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and studied.
</p><p>The D.A. brought Harry into greater contact with <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>. After a meeting, Harry kissed Cho, and when he returned to the Gryffindor Common Room Hermione immediately guessed, asking if Cho had cornered him after the meeting. When Harry told them that Cho has been crying, she explained to Harry and Ron that Cho was having a hard time since <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>, who she used to go out with, was killed by Lord Voldemort. Hermione later gave Harry advice on Cho and girls in general. In an effort to combat the lies being told about Harry, Hermione arranged for an interview during a <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade_weekend_trips" title="Hogsmeade weekend trips">visit</a> with <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> to be printed in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i> telling his side of the story, blackmailing Skeeter into penning it in a sympathetic tone. Despite being banned - or maybe because it was banned - it became the magazine's best-selling issue of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It was Hermione's brilliant spell-work that ensured the security of Dumbledore's Army. She created <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_coin" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army coin">coins</a> enchanted with the <a href="/wiki/Protean_Charm" title="Protean Charm">Protean Charm</a>, an advanced spell, as a method of communication, and <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">jinxed</a> the club's attendance sheet to give any tattler a horrendous rash on the face, which would spell out "<i>SNEAK"</i> in painful boils. This is exactly what happened to <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>, a reluctant member of the D.A., having been brought to the meetings by Cho. Shortly before Easter, Marietta finally caved under the pressure from her ministry mother who worked in the the <a href="/wiki/Floo_Regulation_Panel" title="Floo Regulation Panel">Floo Network Office</a> and betrayed the D.A. to Umbridge. When Harry learned that they could not find a <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curse</a> to heal her face, he swelled with pride at Hermione's jinxing ability.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161216060209" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-image-key="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161216060209" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-image-key="InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161216060209" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:InquistorialSquadOffice.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> are held against their will by the Inquisitorial Squad</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dobby the house-elf learned of this turn of events and rushed to the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> to warn Harry and the D.A. They immediately scattered, and most members escaped, but Harry was caught by Umbridge and several Slytherin students who were members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>. A search of the room uncovered the parchment that each member of the D.A. had signed, headed <i>Dumbledore's Army</i>. Finally having "proof" that Dumbledore was building an army to challenge the Ministry, Umbridge immediately contacted Cornelius Fudge. Dumbledore fled the school and Umbridge became Headmistress. Hermione was not exposed at that time, but later she was brought to Umbridge's office by the some members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Grawp_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160314195015" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Grawp Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Grawp_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Grawp_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160314195015" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Grawp_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160314195015" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Grawp_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160314195015" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Grawp Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Grawp_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Grawp_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160314195015" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grawp_Hermione.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione forcefully telling Grawp to put her down</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Late in the fall of that year, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>, who had been missing for the entirety of the school year, returned to Hogwarts. Hermione, Harry, and Ron ventured down to see him immediately even though it was after curfew. Hermione was aghast at the injuries Hagrid had sustained and greatly curious as to his story. Hagrid told the trio about his mission with <a href="/wiki/Olympe_Maxime" title="Olympe Maxime">Madame Maxime</a> to try and recruit the giants in the fight against Voldemort. They were almost caught when Umbridge called on Hagrid that night, but hid under the Invisibilty Cloak. Months later, Hermione and Harry learned why Hagrid was perpetually bruised and cut; he had brought his giant half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> back to Hogwarts, as he was getting severely bullied, and was trying to teach him human ways. After Grawp, who had the mental age of a human toddler, picked her up, Hermione forcefully told him to put him down. He subsequently became enamoured with Hermione, calling her "Hermy".
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Umbridge%2C_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161002050941" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge, Harry and Hermione in the Forbidden Forest.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge,_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Umbridge%2C_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002050941" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Umbridge%2C_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161002050941" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Umbridge%2C_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002050941" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge, Harry and Hermione in the Forbidden Forest.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge,_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/12/Umbridge%2C_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161002050941" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge,_Harry_and_Hermione_in_the_Forbidden_Forest.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Harry lured Umbridge into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Just after their class took their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.Ls</a>, Harry had a vision of his godfather being tortured by Voldemort in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>. Hermione was worried that it was a trap and convinced Harry to try to contact Sirius before doing anything rash. To that end, she accompanied Harry in an act of solidarity as he sneaked into Umbridge's office to use the <a href="/wiki/Floo_Network" title="Floo Network">Floo Network</a>, with the assistance of Ron, Ginny, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, but they were ultimately caught. When Umbridge threatened to use the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on Harry during questioning, Hermione interceded. She came up with a lie that she and her fellow D.A. members had been building a weapon for Dumbledore, thus stopping Umbridge's sadistic interrogation and attempted torture of Harry.
</p><p>Hermione successfully lured Umbridge into the Forbidden Forest by saying that's where the weapon was hidden, where Umbridge was carried away by a herd of <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a>. She had predicted that the centaurs would let her and Harry go, since they did not insult the centaurs and were young enough to be considered "foals". However, the centaurs were already enraged by Umbridge and were further angered when Hermione admitted that she had hoped that they would drive Umbridge off, being insulted that they were thought of to do the bidding of humans. The centaurs were about to carry the two students off as well, but <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> stumbled onto the scene and a <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Forbidden_Forest" title="Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest">fight broke out</a> between the giant and the herd. This allowed Hermione and Harry to escape and meet up with Ron, Ginny, Luna, and Neville, who had escaped from the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>After a brief argument between Harry and Neville over whether or not the others were going to travel with Harry to London, an understanding was reached. The six students flew on <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> (which the majority, Hermione included, could not even see) to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic_Headquarters" title="British Ministry of Magic Headquarters">Ministry of Magic</a> to try to save Sirius from Voldemort and his Death Eaters.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP Death Chamber trio Ginny Neville Luna.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP Death Chamber trio Ginny Neville Luna.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The six D.A. members battling Death Eaters for possession of the prophecy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione's fear turned out to be justified, as Harry's vision was a ruse planted in his brain by Voldemort designed to lure him to the Ministry to obtain <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">a prophecy</a> Voldemort sought. As soon as Harry did this, the six D.A. members were surrounded by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, and a <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">battle</a> ensued. Hermione <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunned</a> <a href="/wiki/Nott" title="Nott">Nott</a> when he grabbed Harry, thus freeing him and causing Nott to be injured by the <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">collapsing</a> shelves of prophecies. She later stunned another Death Eater and <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silenced</a> <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> before he could alert the other Death Eaters to the group's location. She was critically injured by the <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov%27s_curse" title="Antonin Dolohov&#39;s curse">curse</a> Dolohov subsequently struck her with, but made a full recovery.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sixth_year">Sixth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sixth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Sixth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Its <a href="/wiki/Amortentia" title="Amortentia">Amortentia</a>!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Professor Slughorn</b>: "<i>It is indeed. It seems almost foolish to ask, but I assume you know what it does?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>It's the most powerful love potion in the world... and it's supposed to smell differently to each of us according to what attracts us, and I can smell freshly mown grass and new parchment and —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione possibly realising her feelings towards Ron<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><p>Hermione achieved high academic prestige when she obtained ten <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">Charms</a>, <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a>, <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arithmancy" title="Arithmancy">Arithmancy</a>, <a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Ancient Runes</a>. She received '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' marks on each of them, except Defence Against the Dark Arts in which she received an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>,' which she dwelt upon; Ron found it amusing that she actually seemed disappointed by this.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720150748" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione brewing Draught of Living Death.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720150748" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720150748" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720150748" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione brewing Draught of Living Death.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720150748" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_brewing_Draught_of_Living_Death.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione brewing a <a href="/wiki/Draught_of_Living_Death" title="Draught of Living Death">Draught of Living Death</a> in a N.E.W.T.-level Potions lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By the time they arrived in Hogwarts, Hermione's romantic feelings for Ron had become obvious. According to Harry the two seemed on their way to a romantic relationship. Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>'s relationship suffered greatly in their sixth year, when Ron became envious of both Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, who were invited to be members of the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, a group of students favoured by <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, while he was ignored. Hermione strongly disapproved of Harry using the textbook of the "<a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Half-Blood Prince</a>" to get ahead in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> unfairly, though she did not turn him in and indirectly found a <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">clue</a> about the book owner. She was particularly alarmed by the increasingly Dark nature of the magic in the book, such as the spell <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180305162549" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-harry hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180305162549" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180305162549" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180305162549" decoding="async" width="250" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-harry hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180305162549" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-harry_hermione.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry comforting an upset Hermione after she witnessed Ron snogging Lavender</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, during an argument with his sister, Ginny humiliated Ron about his inexperience with the opposite gender and told him that Hermione had kissed <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> during their earlier romance. Ron subsequently began treating Hermione coldly, much to her bewilderment. She was upset when he and Lavender started flirting. When she found out about Ron's relationship with Lavender, she <a href="/wiki/Bird-Conjuring_Charm" title="Bird-Conjuring Charm">conjured a flock of wild birds</a> to attack Ron for his insensitivity regarding her feelings. He became even angrier with her when she believed that Harry slipped Ron <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a> to assist in his <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>-playing abilities; despite having believed it initially himself, he accused her of having no faith in him when it was discovered that he had not been slipped the potion at all. After this, Hermione attended Slughorn's <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Christmas party</a> with <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a> to get back at Ron, but it did not go well due to the former's impoliteness. Afterwards, Ron (who was relieved that Hermione and McLaggen's date did not go well) attempted to speak to Hermione, but she ignored him, still upset and angry over his previous treatment of her.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> This behaviour presisted for quite sometime.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160830010138" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Poppy Pomfrey - Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160830010138" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160830010138" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160830010138" decoding="async" width="250" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Poppy Pomfrey - Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160830010138" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> checking on a poisoned Ron, while Hermione, Harry, and Ginny are sitting by his bedside</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two reconciled after Ron was hospitalised due to consuming poisoned mead, an event that left Hermione shaken and frightened. After the incident she remained unusually quiet and subdued. Whilst sitting at Ron's bedside, Ron subconsciously muttered Hermione's name. By this time, Ron was visibly disillusioned with his relationship with <a href="/wiki/Lavender" title="Lavender">Lavender</a>, who had become possessive of him and called him by the annoying nickname "<i>Won-Won.</i>" He was also pleased whenever Hermione visited him in the hospital wing. He began avoiding Lavender, who soon became suspicious of his relationship with Hermione, ultimately leading to an argument about her. After Lavender saw Ron and Hermione come down alone from the boys' dormitories (Harry was present also, but under the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a>), she had a fight with Ron and broke up with him. When Ron told Harry and Hermione about breaking up with Lavender, Harry could have sworn he saw Hermione smirk.
</p><p>Afterwards, Hermione and Ron were more comfortable together, and their relationship improved considerably, although a romantic relationship remained out of their reach. Hermione comforted Ron after he failed his <a href="/wiki/Apparition_(class)" title="Apparition (class)">Apparition</a> test because he <a href="/wiki/Splinching" title="Splinching">Splinched</a> half an eyebrow, while he teased her about the <a href="/wiki/Wilkie_Twycross" title="Wilkie Twycross">instructor</a>'s praise for her flawless performance. That year, Hermione also quickly mastered <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbal magic</a>, the first in her class to do so. Throughout the year, Hermione and Ron were both sceptical of Harry's theory that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> had been branded with the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> and was up to something. Moreover, she was confident that Malfoy couldn't have brought any Dark objects into Hogwarts without alerting <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Filch</a>. These claims were heard by Draco himself, who used these details and Hermione's previous plan of communication to accomplish his own.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528011647" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione mourning Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180528011647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528011647" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180528011647" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione mourning Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180528011647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_mourning_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A tearful Hermione standing at the base of the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a> after Dumbledore's death</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Near the end of the school year, Harry's suspicions would be proven right. Malfoy let Death Eaters into the school by means of a pair of vanishing cabinets. One cabinet resided in <a href="/wiki/Borgin_and_Burkes" title="Borgin and Burkes">Borgin and Burkes</a> and the other in the Room of Hidden Things (as it had been presumed broken, but Malfoy managed to fix it). This infiltration of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> resulted in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>. Hermione fought in the battle and remained unscathed thanks to some <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> This was a gift from Harry, who had won it in a Potions competition and had a preconceived notion of what was going to happen. He told Hermione, Ron, and Ginny to drink it beforehand in case his worries proved true.
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The funeral of Albus Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>Throughout the school year, Hermione and Ron had been informed of the content of Harry's private lessons with Dumbledore. Through these lessons Harry, and in turn Hermione and Ron, learned about the existence of Lord Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral</a> of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, who had been killed by Snape in the Battle of the Astronomy Tower, Hermione was comforted by Ron and cried on his shoulder. Afterwards, Harry told them about his desire to drop out of Hogwarts to hunt Horcruxes, which were the key to defeating <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. Despite his protests, Hermione and Ron promised to forgo their seventh year of school in order to assist Harry. Before leaving the school, Hermione was able to <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">Summon</a> books about Horcruxes so as to learn how to destroy the items. She found them in Dumbledore's office, where the late headmaster had kept them after the subject had been banned at Hogwarts.
</p><h3><span id="Horcrux_Hunt_(1997-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Horcrux_Hunt_.281997-1998.29">Horcrux Hunt <span class="template-c">(1997-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Horcrux Hunt (1997-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Horcrux Hunt (1997-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160; Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Listen!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>No, Harry, </i>you<i> listen. We're coming with you. That was decided months ago — years, really.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione sticking by her vow to accompany Harry on his hunt<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160714024300" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory charm.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160714024300" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160714024300" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160714024300" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory charm.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/df/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160714024300" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-memory_charm.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione modifying her parents' memories</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione began planning for her journey with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> immediately. Concerned for the safety of her family, she <a href="/wiki/False_memory_spell" title="False memory spell">altered</a> her parents' memories to make them think they were Wendell and Monica Wilkins and sent them to hide in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, no longer aware of their original identities, the existence of their daughter, or anything she had told them about Harry. She also withdrew all of her savings at her <a href="/wiki/Building_society" title="Building society">building society</a> account, in event of a need for Muggle money.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>. 
</p>
