<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>And then, out of nowhere, out of nothing, they were surrounded. At least thirty <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">hooded figures</a>, suspended in midair, formed a vast circle in the midst of which the Order members had risen, oblivious —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Opening stage of the sky battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106051900" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C4M1 Seven Potters depart.png" data-image-key="B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170106051900" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106051900" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170106051900" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C4M1 Seven Potters depart.png" data-image-key="B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170106051900" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The seven Potters and their protectors right before the sky battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione then joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> in the operation to remove Harry from 4 Privet Drive before his 17th birthday, taking Polyjuice Potion to become one of the "seven Potters". Hermione flew on a <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestral</a> with <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>. The two fought off at least five <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, possibly killing one, injuring two, and were pursued by Lord Voldemort himself at one point. In time, they arrived safely at the<a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow"> Burrow</a>, where Hermione was immensely relieved to see Harry alive and ran to him and hugged him tight, but she was greatly worried when Ron did not show up on time. When he landed, she ran and nuzzled him in relief. She was saddened by the news of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a>'s murders and disturbed by Harry's vision of <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> being <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">tortured</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128225544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Scrimgeour Trio.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128225544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Scrimgeour Trio.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Scrimgeour gives the trio the items left for them in Albus Dumbledore's will</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later on, the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a>, interrupted Harry's birthday celebrations to execute <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Will_and_Testament_of_Albus_Percival_Wulfric_Brian_Dumbledore" title="The Last Will and Testament of Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore's will</a> and bequeath some of his belongings to the three friends. Hermione received <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>, a book of children's stories written in runes. Even before Hermione understood the priceless quality of the gift, she was moved to tears by Dumbledore's great act of friendship. During the reading of Dumbledore's will, she also displayed her incredible store of general knowledge when she mentioned that "<i>Snitches have flesh memories,</i>" surprising both Ron and Harry, who had both believed her to know little to nothing of <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>.
</p><p>At Bill Weasley and Fleur Delacour's <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> on 1 August, 1997, Hermione wore a "<i>floaty, lilac-coloured dress with matching high heels</i>" and made her hair "<i>sleek and shiny.</i>" She was amused by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>'s stories about their late uncle <a href="/wiki/Bilius" title="Bilius">Bilius</a> and shared a friendly exchange with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, to the frustration of Ron. She was happily surprised when Ron quickly asked her to dance, and when Krum asked a disguised Harry whether the two were together, Harry replied "<i>Er... sort of.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Time_at_the_Burrow">Time at the Burrow</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Time at the Burrow">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Time at the Burrow"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Undetectable Extension Charm. Tricky, but I think I've done it okay; anyway, I managed to fit everything we need in here... I told you at the Burrow, I've had the essentials packed for days, you know, in case we needed to make a quick getaway.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione has the foresight to have supplies packed in advance<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310235219" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180310235219" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310235219" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180310235219" decoding="async" width="245" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180310235219" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-part-i-20100922043334092.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kingsley's <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> warning the wedding attendees of the Ministry's fall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The wedding was interrupted by Kingsley Shacklebolt's Patronus who told the guests of the fall of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Hermione was prepared to make a quick escape, immediately Disapparating herself, Harry, and Ron away from the danger. Hermione also showed great foresight and magical talent when she revealed a small beaded purse on which she had placed an <a href="/wiki/Extension_Charm" title="Extension Charm">Undetectable Extension Charm</a>. Within it she had packed, amongst other things, clothing, a tent, healing supplies, Harry's <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a>, and several useful books. They arrived on the Muggle street, <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Court_Road" title="Tottenham Court Road">Tottenham Court Road</a>, where Hermione suggested they enter a café, as a means to get out of the open.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140907215707" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione duelling Dolohov.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140907215707" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140907215707" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140907215707" decoding="async" width="241" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione duelling Dolohov.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/01/Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20140907215707" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_duelling_Dolohov.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione casting <i>Petrificus Totalus</i> on Antonin Dolohov</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, minutes later Hermione unknowingly triggered the <a href="/wiki/Taboo" title="Taboo">Taboo curse</a> that was placed on Voldemort's name, and the trio were thus tracked down by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>. After a brief but violent <a href="/wiki/Luchino_Caffe_Duel" title="Luchino Caffe Duel">skirmish</a>, the Death Eaters were subdued, and Hermione modified their memories to throw them off the scent and to maintain Ron's cover story that he was sick with <a href="/wiki/Spattergroit" title="Spattergroit">spattergroit</a> and bedridden at home. At Harry's suggestion the three then made their way safely to 12 Grimmauld Place, as they could not hide anywhere within the wizarding world.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Infiltrating_the_Ministry_of_Magic">Infiltrating the Ministry of Magic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Infiltrating the Ministry of Magic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Infiltrating the Ministry of Magic"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>This is mental.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Completely mental.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The trio's mutual feelings on the infiltration plan<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>After learning from <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a> that Dolores Umbridge had Tom Riddle's mother's locket - one of the seven Horcruxes - in her possession, the trio formed a plan to infiltrate the Ministry and reclaim the locket. Hermione imbibed Polyjuice Potion and transformed to look like <a href="/wiki/Mafalda_Hopkirk" title="Mafalda Hopkirk">Mafalda Hopkirk</a>, a prominent Ministry official. She was forced to sit through the trials of <a href="/wiki/Alderton" title="Alderton">Alderton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>, innocent Muggle-borns, right alongside Umbridge and Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a>. Hermione tricked Umbridge into telling her about the locket, which she claimed was a Selwyn family heirloom.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180424032414" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter&#39;s Patronus saving Marry Cattermole.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter&#39;s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180424032414" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180424032414" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180424032414" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter&#39;s Patronus saving Marry Cattermole.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter&#39;s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180424032414" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter%27s_Patronus_saving_Marry_Cattermole.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry casting his Patronus at <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> while in the trial courtroom, before capturing the locket</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry attacked Umbridge in a rage, their cover was blown, but she and Harry managed to free the Muggle-born prisoners and encouraged them to flee the country while Voldemort was in power. Hermione took the locket from Umbridge, replacing it with a copy using the <a href="/wiki/Doubling_Charm" title="Doubling Charm">Geminio</a> spell. They met up with Ron again and fled the Ministry, but Yaxley grabbed onto Hermione's arm while they were Disapparating. This meant that he was unwittingly brought inside the enchantment making Grimmauld Place undetectable, and forced Hermione to use a <a href="/wiki/Revulsion_Jinx" title="Revulsion Jinx">Revulsion Jinx</a> to free herself from him, and then to take the trio away from Grimmauld Place.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Ron's_departure_and_Godric's_Hollow"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron.27s_departure_and_Godric.27s_Hollow">Ron's departure and Godric's Hollow</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron&#039;s departure and Godric&#039;s Hollow">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Ron&#039;s departure and Godric&#039;s Hollow"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>What are you doing? Are you staying, or what?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>I... Yes — yes, I'm staying. Ron, we said we'd go with Harry, we said we'd help —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I get it. You choose him.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Ron, no — please — come back, come back!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione keeping her promise to Harry shortly before Ron's departure<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry_ron_fight.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140905115741" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry ron fight.gif" data-image-key="Harry_ron_fight.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry_ron_fight.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140905115741" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry_ron_fight.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140905115741" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry_ron_fight.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140905115741" decoding="async" width="240" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry ron fight.gif" data-image-key="Harry_ron_fight.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/75/Harry_ron_fight.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140905115741" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_ron_fight.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Ron row before Ron abandons the hunt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The locket caused great pain among the three friends due to the negative energy within. They began arguing over petty issues such as cooking, and growing moodier. The negative energy from the locket caused Ron to accuse Harry of poor leadership. They fought physically, although Hermione stopped them before they started casting spells by casting a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> between them. Ron also accused Hermione of choosing Harry over him, causing him to be jealous and feel left out by his two friends' growing friendship. He declared he was leaving and stormed out of the tent.
</p><p>By the time she got rid of the shield charm, all Hermione could do was scream for him to come back, without success. Hermione then cried over Ron for more than a week after his departure, although she tried to hide it from Harry. Both were deeply saddened and hurt by their friend's departure, although Hermione more than Harry, as she cried over Ron's departure for weeks. With Ron gone, Hermione and Harry's evenings were spent in mostly silence, while they contemplated Ron's abandonment and the places Voldemort's remaining Horcruxes might be hidden.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310232353" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione godric&#39;s hollow.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_godric&#39;s_hollow.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310232353" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310232353" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310232353" decoding="async" width="250" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione godric&#39;s hollow.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_godric&#39;s_hollow.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310232353" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_godric%27s_hollow.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione in Bathilda Bagshot's cottage, holding the <i><a href="/wiki/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore">The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione and Harry soon decided to go to <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>, to see the graves of Harry's parents and to speak to historian <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>. They believed Bathilda might be holding onto <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a> for Harry, as they thought Dumbledore might have left it with her as an old family friend, knowing it was the only method the trio knew for destroying a Horcrux. Hermione comforted Harry in the graveyard when they found the <a href="/wiki/James_and_Lily_Potter%27s_grave" title="James and Lily Potter&#39;s grave">Potters' graves</a>; she nuzzled her head in to the crook between his head and shoulders and conjured roses for the graves. On their way out of the graveyeard they came into contact with what appeared to be Bathilda. The pair then went to Bathilda's house; whilst in the house they were separated. Harry was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> upstairs, who had been waiting for them in the guise of the old woman, whose corpse had been animated like an <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferius</a> by Voldemort. Hermione rushed to Harry's aid and proceeded to save his life, and the two of them barely escaped before Lord Voldemort himself arrived at the cabin in an attempt to capture Harry.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160303145232" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160303145232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160303145232" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160303145232" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3e/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160303145232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-10950.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Hermione talking about Albus Dumbledore in the forest of Dean</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparated</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Dean" title="Forest of Dean">Forest of Dean</a>, while Harry was overcome with pain and visions of Voldemort's attack on his parents and him in 1981. She used a <a href="/wiki/Severing_Charm" title="Severing Charm">Severing Charm</a> to remove the locket from Harry and healed the bite Nagini had given him with dittany. Harry's wand had also been broken in the foray, most likely by the <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">Blasting Curse</a> Hermione cast at Nagini. Hermione was very upset a the thought that it was her curse that broke Harry's wand. Harry was heartbroken, but not angry with her, knowing that it was an accident and that Hermione had saved his life and therefore could not hold it against her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Ron's_return_and_visit_to_the_Lovegood_House"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron.27s_return_and_visit_to_the_Lovegood_House">Ron's return and visit to the Lovegood House</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron&#039;s return and visit to the Lovegood House">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Ron&#039;s return and visit to the Lovegood House"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Hand over Harry?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>No deal, get out of the way, we're leaving.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron refuse to hand Harry over to Voldemort<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Harry and Hermione were reunited with Ron in the Forest of Dean, after Ron heard them talking through the <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a> Dumbledore had left to him. Ron destroyed the locket Horcrux with Godric Gryffindor's Sword, which had been left by an unknown assistant in a pool in the Forest, saving Harry's life and thus receiving forgiveness from Harry for leaving. Before he destroyed it, however, the locket revealed some of Ron's deepest fears, including that Hermione preferred Harry to him. Hermione, however, was unaware of this, as she had been in the tent while this occurred. Upon seeing Ron, she screamed at Ron despite Harry trying to tell her that Ron just saved his life, and punched him until Harry cast a shield charm between them with Hermione's wand. She was furious with Ron for days for his abandonment, but gradually warmed up to him again.
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Ambush_at_the_Lovegood_House" title="Ambush at the Lovegood House">Ambush at the Lovegood House</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest?cb=20141031144607" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-image-key="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest?cb=20141031144607" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-image-key="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio speaking with Xenophilius Lovegood at his home, near the village of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The trio then travelled together to <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a>'s home to ask him about the strange symbol in <i>The Tales of Beedle the Bard, </i>which Xenophilius had worn on a chain around his neck at Bill and Fleur's wedding. They had thought it to be the sign of the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a> after Krum recognised it at the wedding (Grindelwald being a former Durmstrang student), but Xenophilius informed them it was the symbol of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. Shortly after making this discovery, Harry realised that Luna wasn't at home, despite it being the Christmas holidays, and had been away for a long time. Xenophilius revealed to them that Luna had been taken prisoner by Death Eaters and that he planned to betray them in order to get her back.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160601024538" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="249" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ambush at Lovegood house1.jpg" data-image-key="Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20160601024538" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160601024538" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20160601024538" decoding="async" width="249" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ambush at Lovegood house1.jpg" data-image-key="Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/da/Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20160601024538" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ambush_at_Lovegood_house1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Death Eaters ambush the trio while they're inside the Lovegood home</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, in attempting to capture them, Xenophilius made the <a href="/wiki/Erumpent" title="Erumpent">Erumpent</a> horn in his living room (which he had insisted was a Snorkack horn, much to Hermione's annoyance) explode, giving the trio the chance to hide just as Death Eaters <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a> arrived. They threatened to kill Luna if they found that Xenophilius had lied about Harry Potter's presence in his home. In a remarkable show of mental and magical dexterity, Hermione concocted the trio's escape while safeguarding Ron's feigned illness and allowing the Death Eaters to glimpse Harry, so that they would not carry out their threat to kill Luna.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You're lying, filthy Mudblood, and I know it! You have been inside my vault at Gringotts!... What else did you take? Tell me the truth or, I swear, I shall run you through with this knife! What else did you take, what else? ANSWER ME! </i>CRUCIO<i>! How did you get into my vault? Did that dirty little <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">goblin</a> in the cellar help you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Overheard parts of Hermione's brutal interrogation<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>In the spring of 1998, Harry accidentally triggered the Taboo curse and Hermione, Harry, and Ron were tracked down and captured by a group of <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a>, which included the <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Greyback had developed cannibalistic tendencies when out of werewolf form and was eager to bite Hermione. After a brief and violent interrogation by the Snatchers, the captives were brought to Malfoy Manor and turned over to <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Bellatrix immediately panicked at the sight of Godric Gryffindor's Sword and incapacitated the Snatchers with ease, as she was too quick for them. She then ordered them moved to the courtyard where she would deal with them later.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c5/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170717220831" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="248" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c5/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/248?cb=20170717220831" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c5/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170717220831" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c5/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/248?cb=20170717220831" decoding="async" width="248" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c5/Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/248?cb=20170717220831" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-deathly-hallows1-movie-screencaps.com-14694.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bellatrix torturing Hermione</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix gave away that what she believed to be the sword and another Horcrux were hidden in her vault at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> in her panic. She proceeded to isolate Hermione and then brutally torture her with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> repeatedly along with taking a dagger and cutting the word Mudblood into her arm as interrogation methods. Ron (who had tried to take her place unsuccessfully) was reduced to sobs from hearing Hermione scream in pain. However, Hermione came up with a fake story that the sword was merely a copy of the real thing; a lie that Harry persuaded the imprisoned goblin <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a> to go along with. Hermione was soon tortured into unconsciousness. With Hermione's moans and screams of pain echoing throughout the manor, Harry and Ron saw no possible hope left. Suddenly, <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> came to the rescue of the prisoners in the dungeon, with audible crack as he apparated. Harry and Ron fought off <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, who had been sent to investigate the noise. Harry snarled at him that Pettigrew owed him for Harry's sparing of his life with Lupin and Sirius, and the momentary relaxing of Pettigrew as a result caused him to be choked to death by his own silver hand (created by Voldemort) for showing Harry mercy. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811153316" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811153316" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811153316" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811153316" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/db/Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811153316" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix-x-Hermione-bellatrix-and-hermione-27355000-1280-528.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bellatrix holds her silver knife to Hermione's throat</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They raced upstairs and were forced to drop their wands when Bellatrix held a silver knife to Hermione's throat. Bellatrix cut through some skin, leaving a thin cut on the front of Hermoine's neck. Right when Bellatrix was about to slit her throat, <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> returned and sent the chandelier crashing to the floor, knocking Bellatrix over and enabling Harry to grab their wands from Draco and <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Disapparate</a> with Hermione, Ron, Griphook, and Dobby to <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>, where Bill and Fleur Weasley took up residence after their marriage. Unfortunately, Dobby was killed during this escape, by a knife Bellatrix threw.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shell_Cottage_and_Gringotts_break-in">Shell Cottage and Gringotts break-in</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Shell Cottage and Gringotts break-in">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Shell Cottage and Gringotts break-in"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Griphook</b>: "<i>As the Dark Lord becomes ever more powerful, your race is set still more firmly above mine! <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a> falls under wizarding rule, house-elves are slaughtered, and who amongst the wand-carriers protests?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>We do! We protest!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione shows her willingness to stand up for others<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811141202" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="249" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-shell cottage.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180811141202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811141202" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180811141202" decoding="async" width="249" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-shell cottage.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/16/Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20180811141202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-shell_cottage.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio speaking with <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a> about what lies within the Lestrange vault at Gringotts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione, Harry, and Ron stayed at Shell Cottage for some time, whilst Fleur helped Hermione recover from her trauma. Ron didn't leave Hermione's bedside throughout this time. The trio formed a plan to break into the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Vault" title="Lestrange Vault">Lestrange Vault</a> at Gringotts to retrieve the Horcrux <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Helga Hufflepuff's Cup</a>, with the reluctant assistance of Griphook. The goblin only agreed to help them in exchange for Gryffindor's Sword; although lothe to lose it, Hermione was strongly against deceiving or double-crossing Griphook, who was startled by the care she and Harry had shown for house-elves,since most wizards do not think highly of non-human beings. The trio reluctantly agreed to Griphook's terms.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310225013" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Break-in 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Break-in_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310225013" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310225013" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310225013" decoding="async" width="250" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Break-in 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Break-in_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310225013" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Break-in_1998.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione, disguised as Dragomir Despard and <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once more, Hermione used Polyjuice Potion, containing Bellatrix's hair. She was also forced to use <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange%27s_first_wand" title="Bellatrix Lestrange&#39;s first wand">Bellatrix's wand</a>, as her wand had been confiscated by <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a>. She very much disliked this, as the wand in question had caused so much suffering, such as contributing to Sirius' murder. She stated that the wand felt wrong and Harry speculated that it was because Hermione had not won the wand's intelligence.
</p><p>It was determined that Hermione was "too polite" to really impersonate Bellatrix, a she did not treat those around her like scum. Despite this, the group managed to get into the vault, mainly because of Harry's use of the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>. After many harrowing challenges, and Griphook betraying them out of a belief that they would not have kept to their agreement. Hermione, Ron, and Harry escaped on the back of the <a href="/wiki/Dragon" title="Dragon">half-blind dragon</a> that was guarding the vault, with another Horcrux in their possession.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Oi! There's a war going on here!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I know, mate, so it's now or never, isn't it?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron share a passionate kiss during the final battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108173526" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108173526" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108173526" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108173526" decoding="async" width="251" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108173526" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron destroying the cup in the Chamber of Secrets</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The trio finally returned to Hogwarts on 2 May, 1998, with the assistance of <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, after Harry had a vision that the remaining Horcrux they had not identified (but suspected was something formerly belonging to <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a>) was hidden at the school. They were reunited with their friends in the reformed Dumbledore's Army, who declared their wish to fight the encroaching Death Eater army. Whilst Harry and Luna went to Ravenclaw Tower, Hermione and Ron retrieved <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">basilisk</a> fangs from the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> in order to use them to destroy Horcruxes, and Hermione destroyed <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" title="Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Hufflepuff's Cup</a>.
</p><p>Soon after reuniting with Harry, Ron expressed concern for the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a> in the Hogwarts kitchens, prompting Hermione to kiss him for the very first time. Ron responded with great enthusiasm, but they quickly broke apart when Harry reminded them of their objective.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140308202617" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fiend fyre Fleeing GIF.gif" data-image-key="Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140308202617" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" decoding="async" width="245" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fiend fyre Fleeing GIF.gif" data-image-key="Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron run from the towering flames of <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">Fiendfyre</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The trio then entered the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> in search for Rowena Ravenclaw's <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" title="Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Diadem</a>, but were ambushed by <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>. Hermione dodged a <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a> and managed to stun Goyle, and then she and Ron dragged him out of the room on a broomstick as it went up in flames due to Crabbe's cursed <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">Fiendfyre</a>, which also destroyed the Horcrux. Harry rescued Draco, but Crabbe was killed by his creation. 
</p><p>Harry, Hermione and Ron then witnessed the death of <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a>, which devastated them all. Despite their grief, the trio continued with the effort to track down Nagini, the last Horcrux (that they knew of). On their way, Hermione incapacitated two <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who were pursuing her, Harry and Ron, and blasted <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> away from an injured <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>. Lavender unfortunately still tragically died afterwards from her injuries.
</p><p>The trio was swarmed by Dementors and all had difficulty summoning their Patronuses because of the horror of their recent experiences, but Luna, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Macmillan" title="Ernest Macmillan">Ernie Macmillan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a> came to their assistance. Under Harry's Invisibility Cloak, the three made their way to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, where they witnessed Voldemort have Nagini kill Severus Snape, as he had (ultimately incorrectly) assumed that the Elder Wand's loyalty lay with Snape.
</p><p>During the brief pause in fighting, when Voldemort issued an ultimatum to Harry, Hermione comforted <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> over Fred's death. When Voldemort and his army approached with a supposedly dead Harry, Hermione screamed in horror and denial.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione witnesses Harry's final defeat of Lord Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Battle of Hogwarts soon resumed, and Hermione fought <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> alongside Ginny and Luna, despite being hindered by using Bellatrix's own wand against her. When Bellatrix nearly killed Ginny, <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> took over the fight and killed Bellatrix. Hermione witnessed Harry's final defeat of Lord Voldemort, and she and Ron reached him first, overjoyed. Hermione survived the battle relatively unscathed, only suffering minor injuries and burns she received from entering the Lestranges' Vault shortly before the battle.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Later_life_(1998-2020)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Later_life_.281998-2020.29">Later life <span class="template-c">(1998-2020)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-2020)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Later life (1998-2020)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>At some point Hermione found her parents in Australia and restored their memories. In 1998, Hermione went back to Hogwarts to attain her <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> She was the only one of the trio to do this, and by 2017 (nineteen years later) Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> were married with two children: <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo Granger-Weasley</a>. Hermione is also the godmother of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Potter</a>'s eldest child, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ministry_of_Magic_employee">Ministry of Magic employee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ministry of Magic employee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Ministry of Magic employee"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Bloomsbury Live Chat">"<i>Hermione began her post-Hogwarts career at the Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures where she was instrumental in greatly improving life for house-elves and their ilk. She then moved (despite her jibe to Scrimgeour) to the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a> where she was a progressive voice who ensured the eradication of oppressive, pro-pureblood laws.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> regarding Hermione's future<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Bloomsbury_Live_Chat" title="Bloomsbury Live Chat">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811150508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811150508" decoding="async" width="251" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180811150508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A 37-year-old Hermione with her family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione attained a high position in the Ministry of Magic, first through the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_the_Regulation_and_Control_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures">Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures</a>. There, she continued her work with <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">S.P.E.W.</a>, working for the rights of underprivileged non-humans such as house-elves. She then went on to become Deputy Head<sup id="cite_ref-dumbledores-army-reunites_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dumbledores-army-reunites-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement, and assisted the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> in eradicating the old laws biased in favour of <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-bloods</a>.
</p><p>Along with Harry and Ron, she helped to revolutionise the Ministry and reform the wizarding world. At some point, Hermione, Harry, and Ron were all featured on <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Cards</a> for their accomplishments.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hermione also eventually translated <i>The Tales of Beedle the Bard</i> from the original, which had been written in runes and which <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> bequeathed to her in his will in 1997. Her new translation was published in 2008 and included notes on each tale written by Dumbledore before his death; these notes were lent to Hermione by her former professor, Hogwarts headmistress <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 241px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813031055" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="239" height="122" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione &amp; Ron with their children at platform nine and three quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_&amp;_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20140813031055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813031055" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20140813031055" decoding="async" width="239" height="122" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione &amp; Ron with their children at platform nine and three quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_&amp;_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/239?cb=20140813031055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione with her husband and children</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Both Hermione and Ron attended the <a href="/wiki/2014_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="2014 Quidditch World Cup">2014 Quidditch World Cup</a> and sat in VIP Box Two. Rita Skeeter noted that Ron had become catatonic at the appearance of the Bulgarian Veela and Hermione had to elbow him in the ribs.
</p><p>On 1 September, <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Hermione and Ron brought their children to <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a> to see Rose off for her first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>, and met Harry, Ginny, and their three children there.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a>, Hermione acted as one of the apparent leading members of the newly-created <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> and would introduce members who had proven to be qualified to Professions after complimenting on their impressive combination of determination and ability. She would also help the members personally, instructing those who pursued a professorship on the Proficiency Charm after returning from a sojourn overseas while giving Aurors a retrospective regarding her experiences in the Second Wizarding War to help them in fighting Death Eaters.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Minister_for_Magic">Minister for Magic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minister for Magic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Minister for Magic"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sometime before <a href="/wiki/2019" title="2019">2019</a>, Hermione became the new <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>. Given elections generally occur every seven years, and Shacklebolt was appointed in 1997, it is likely that his first election took place shortly thereafter. If Shacklebolt was elected in 1998 or 1999, subsequent seven-year terms would suggest Granger was first elected Minister in 2012–13 or 2019.
</p><p>In the summer of <a href="/wiki/2020" title="2020">2020</a>, Hermione had to visit Harry to ask him to complete his paperwork and the other tasks he was yet to do. She talked about her concerns for recent activity similar to ones which happened when Voldemort was alive. Harry reminded her that he did just find a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> and he would get round to the rest of the tasks in his own time. They agreed that the Time-Turner should be destroyed and Hermione hid it away.
</p><p>A few months later, Hermione was returning to her office when she was stopped by Ron, who was really <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> transfigured to look like Ron. Albus was trying to stall her while <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphi</a> stole the Time-Turner. Hermione found Ron annoying although he stalled her long enough for the others to find the Time-Turner and they left.
</p><p>Hermione had found out about Harry's nightmares and how his scar was hurting again and she called a meeting. However, no one thought it was a threat.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 246px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802193002" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="244" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Hermione cursed child.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20160802193002" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802193002" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20160802193002" decoding="async" width="244" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Hermione cursed child.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20160802193002" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron standing in her office at the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione's life was changed by Albus and Scorpius when they meddled with time. In one <a href="/wiki/Alternate_reality" title="Alternate reality">alternate reality</a>, she did not marry Ron and became the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. In another alternate reality where Harry died, Hermione was in hiding as a member of what remained of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> with Ron and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. When Scorpius turned up with information about the original timeline where they won, Hermione agreed to help put time right again by time-travelling to the moment Scorpius changed time and use a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> to stop him. Hermione was the one to use the charm first, but when they returned to the present, it was still changed. They were attacked by Dementors and Hermione and Ron professed their love for each other and sacrificed their souls to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> to give Scorpius time to escape.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190719140007" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload"
