data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190719140007" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190719140007" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190719140007" decoding="async" width="220" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy. 1537-1140x800.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2d/The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190719140007" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-Australian-company-of-Harry-Potter-and-the-Cursed-Child.-Photo-Matt-Murphy._1537-1140x800.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione Granger as a Defence Against the Dark Arts professor in the alternate timeline</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When time was right again, Hermione visited Hogwarts to attend a meeting with Professor McGonagall. Hermione, along with Ron, Harry, Ginny and Draco were very forgiving of what Albus and Scorpius did, but McGonagall reminded them of great dangers that happened, and could still have been, because they meddled with time.
</p><p>When Albus and Scorpius were kidnapped by Delphi and made to travel in time again to <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">October 31</a> <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>, Hermione travelled in time again with Ron, Harry, Ginny and Draco Malfoy to save them. Hermione helped transfigure Harry to look like Voldemort to trick Delphi who hopes to save him, and then later helped Harry duel Delphi. She and Draco then apprehended her and took her back to the present where she was sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190117041925" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Granger OOTP profile.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190117041925" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Granger OOTP profile.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione in her fifth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Hermione_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070807224210" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione yule ball.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_yule_ball.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Hermione_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070807224210" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Hermione_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070807224210" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Hermione_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070807224210" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione yule ball.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_yule_ball.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Hermione_yule_ball.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20070807224210" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_yule_ball.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione in her Yule Ball dress robes during her fourth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione had light skin, bright brown eyes, lots of bushy brown hair (once described as a <i>"long mane of brown hair"</i>),<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and — as a child — rather large front teeth.<sup id="cite_ref-hair_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hair-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-eyes_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eyes-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>  She possessed a sort of bossy voice that would become slightly shrill when she was angry.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hermione generally wore her school uniform under her robes. Otherwise, she dressed casually. She usually kept her hair long and sometimes tied it back in a plait.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hermione never gave much attention to her appearance, usually hiding her potential to be considered extremely pretty under her bushy hairstyle and a large pile of books, which she kept slung on her back.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> magically <a href="/wiki/Tooth-shrinking_spell" class="mw-redirect" title="Tooth-shrinking spell">shrunk</a> her front teeth after she was accidentally struck with a <i><a href="/wiki/Densaugeo" title="Densaugeo">Densaugeo</a></i> spell, and told Hermione to alert her when her teeth had returned to their original size. Hermione deviously let the spell continue a little longer, making it unnecessary for her to receive the braces her parents - both dentists - had originally intended for her. 
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, Hermione revealed that when she put her mind to it, she could look truly beautiful - she used <a href="/wiki/Sleekeazy%27s_Hair_Potion" title="Sleekeazy&#39;s Hair Potion">Sleekeazy's Hair Potion</a> to fix her hair, making it sleek and shiny, and twisted up into an elegant knot at the back of her head. She wore robes made of a floaty, periwinkle-blue material, and she held herself differently. Harry himself failed to recognise her initially, and was shocked when he did, for she didn't look at all like her usual self. Even Pansy Parkinson gaped at Hermione when she saw her, and Draco seemed unable to find an insult to throw at her.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> A similar transformation was seen during the wedding of Bill and Fleur - her hair was again <i>"sleek and shiny"</i>, and she wore a floaty, lilac-coloured dress with matching high heels.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;After Hermione impresses &#91;&#91;Horace Slughorn&#124;Slughorn&#93;&#93; with her knowledge"><b>Horace Slughorn</b>: "<i>Oho! 'One of my best friends is Muggle-born, and she's the best in our year!' I'm assuming this is the very friend of whom you spoke, Harry?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Yes, sir.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Horace Slughorn</b>: "<i>Well, well, take 20 well-earned points for Gryffindor, Miss Granger.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Did you really tell him I’m the best in the year? Oh, Harry!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; After Hermione impresses <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a> with her knowledge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_reading.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310235724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione reading.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_reading.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_reading.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310235724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_reading.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310235724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_reading.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310235724" decoding="async" width="246" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione reading.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_reading.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Hermione_reading.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310235724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_reading.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione was known to read for recreation and for fun</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was noted for being both extremely intellectual curious and very hard-working, coming out on top in most of her classes and continuously aiding Harry and Ron in their adventures. She was so studious that the Ministry allowed her a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> in her third year, a device that rewinds time so that she could take extra courses.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Because of her efficiency and compassion, Hermione often had time to do hobby work on the side, such as preparing a defence for <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> to save him from execution and creating <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">S.P.E.W.</a>, an organisation promoting the freedom of <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Such acts demonstrated her social conscience and tenacity.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>That's what Hermione does. When in doubt, go to the library.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's opinion of Hermione's personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080515230612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="273" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione with her Hand Up.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080515230612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080515230612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080515230612" decoding="async" width="180" height="273" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione with her Hand Up.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080515230612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_with_her_Hand_Up.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione's enthusiasm in class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unlike most wizards who depended solely on their magical ability, Hermione readily relied on logic, which often helped her to cleverly deduce information that many others missed, such as <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">lycanthropy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> However, her emphasis on logic made her sceptical about accepting anything without proof, as opposed to Harry who would come to intuitive conclusions, such as completely dismissing the idea of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>, refusing to believe in them without physical evidence.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hermione's logic has limits, putting her beliefs before all else at the same time in a way that makes her ignore reality when it contradicts what she believes, no matter how strong or overwhelming the evidence is. An example of this is the reality of the house-elves, insisting that they wanted to be free, have wages and only seemed happy because they were under educated and brainwashed, even though her friends and the elves themselves told her they were happy and didn't want her help because they don't usually think the way humans do.
</p><p>Hermione was quite blunt with her opinions, sometimes to the point of being tactless. For example, her attempt to comfort <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a> about the death of her rabbit didn't go over well,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and her honesty when dealing with <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a> in 1996 nearly landed her and Harry in serious trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Despite this, Hermione was generally sensitive to others' emotions and would lie when she had to, though she wasn't a skilled liar.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She also gave her friends advice rather often, such as in trying to make Harry understand Cho Chang's behaviour on their date,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> and in helping Ginny deal with her crush on Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> These actions once prompted Ron to advise her to write a book to translate all the "mad things" girls do so that boys could understand them.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Hermione's immense workload finally seemed to be getting to her. Every night, without fail, Hermione was to be seen in a corner of the common room, several tables spread with books, <a href="/wiki/Arithmancy_(class)" title="Arithmancy (class)">Arithmancy</a> charts, rune dictionaries, diagrams of Muggles lifting heavy objects, and file upon file of extensive notes; she barely spoke to anybody and snapped when she was interrupted.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione's intense workload starts to weight on her<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hermione was very responsible, a strict perfectionist and well put-together who often attempted to act as the voice of reason among her more impulsive friends, to varying levels of success. These traits led to her being made a prefect during her fifth year. Throughout her entire school career, Hermione was insistent on order and steadfastly devoted to the rules, often at the expense of her popularity. Her sense of humour was limited, frequently expressing disapproval over <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>'s practical jokes and threatened to put them in detention for selling prank items in the common room.  
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081029220506" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg" data-image-key="TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20081029220506" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081029220506" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20081029220506" decoding="async" width="241" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg" data-image-key="TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e5/TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20081029220506" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:TrioCommonRoomHBP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione arguing with Harry Potter over the Half-blood Prince's copy of <i>Advanced Potion-Making</i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was very determined and focused, in that she "<i>always [kept] her attention focused on the job that must be done</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Her refusal to break under torture shows her strength of willpower.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She wasn't afraid to stand up to her friends when she thought it was in their best interests, or when she felt they were wrong; risking to anger Harry by getting his <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Firebolt" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Firebolt">Firebolt</a> confiscated because she feared it might be jinxed,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and arguing with both him and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> over his use of the shady Half Blood Prince's textbook.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In spite of her strait-laced disposition, she wasn't above using coercion and threats to get what she wanted, achieve results or protect herself and those she cared about in the long run. This is evidenced by her blackmailing Rita Skeeter into writing a good article about Harry<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>, as well as slapping Draco Malfoy when he insulted Hagrid and drawing her wand on him, using a Confundus Charm on Cormac McLaggen for insulting her friends and placing a jinx on the list of DA members that would cause them to sprout boils all over their face in the word "SNEAK" if they betrayed the organisation. Malfoy, Rita Skeeter and Marietta Edgecombe all served as examples of what could result if they pushed the most talented witch of her generation one inch too far. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>I'm hunted quite as much as any <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">goblin</a> or elf, Griphook! I'm a Mudblood!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Don't call yourself —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Why shouldn't I? I am a Mudblood, and proud of it!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione expressing pride at being a Muggle-born<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 238px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110714002806" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="236" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20110714002806" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110714002806" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20110714002806" decoding="async" width="236" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/72/Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20110714002806" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione-granger-ron-weasley-harry-potter-hp4-study-6x4.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione urging Harry and Ron to take studying seriously</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Because of her opinionated, interfering nature, Hermione had the reputation for being a bossy know-it-all. Her sometimes abrasive attitude masked deep insecurities and fear of failure, as personified by her <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-JKRHG_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JKRHG-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> She felt the need to prove herself, perhaps partly because of how many people in wizarding society looked down on Muggle-borns. However, she didn't let anyone bully her about this and ignored bigots like Draco Malfoy. Despite her growing confidence in her abilities, Hermione wasn't arrogant or conceited, and helped her classmates with their schoolwork whenever she could. In her fifth year, she also became one of the few people to call Voldemort by name.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though she initially showed a tendency toward mild panic in sudden situations,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> in time she was able to overcome this trait of hers, and demonstrated her bravery and extreme loyalty to her friends many times when facing danger, risking her life frequently to help them and standing by Harry even when no one else did. Although she wasn't as short-tempered as her friends, Hermione displayed a formidable fury on several occasions, such as slapping Draco Malfoy in defence of Hagrid,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> sabotaging Cormac McLaggen's tryout as a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> after he insulted Ron and Ginny, conjuring a flock of canaries to attack Ron in their sixth year<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and physically attacking him when he briefly abandoned her and Harry during their hunt for Horcruxes.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She also tended to be rather argumentative, a trait most evident in her interactions with Ron.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 218px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f3/Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png/revision/latest?cb=20170109003508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="216" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Otter Patronus.png" data-image-key="Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f3/Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/216?cb=20170109003508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f3/Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png/revision/latest?cb=20170109003508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f3/Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/216?cb=20170109003508" decoding="async" width="216" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Otter Patronus.png" data-image-key="Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f3/Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/216?cb=20170109003508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Otter_Patronus.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione's corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> (form of an otter)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>An' they haven't invented a spell our Hermione can' do.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> praising Hermione's outstanding magical talents<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hermione proved to be an extremely powerful and talented young witch. Even before she began her education at Hogwarts, she practised some simple spells which all worked.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> claimed that Hermione was the cleverest witch of her age he had ever met.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Her magical capability easily surpassed almost every single student in her year, challenged only by a select few.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>One of my best friends is Muggle-born, and she's the best in our year.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> addressing Hermione's magical aptitude<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> aptitude</b>: At Hogwarts, Hermione was usually the first to master any spell and could use spells beyond her educational level.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She earned ten <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>; nine '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstandings</a>', and one '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>', in <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. Harry Potter was the strongest student in that subject,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> but even Harry acknowledged that Hermione was "the best in our year," and repeatedly admired her spell work.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">nonverbal magic</a></b>: Hermione became highly skilled at <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">non-verbal magic</a> in her sixth year, being the first to succeed at it in her <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class and quickly becoming so good at non-verbal <a href="/wiki/Incantation" title="Incantation">incantations</a> that she did not need to say the incantations aloud for a wide variety of <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> She was known to have practised <a href="/wiki/Wandless_magic" title="Wandless magic">wandless magic</a> in her years at Hogwarts. Hermione did not need the aid of a <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a> or magical instrument for a wide variety of spells.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Neville, I'm really sorry about this. Petrificus Totalus!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione's use of the <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> in her first year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110926233856" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="67" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron casting Stupefy.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110926233856" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110926233856" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110926233856" decoding="async" width="180" height="67" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron casting Stupefy.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110926233856" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron casting the <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> at <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140307044201" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione blasting Greyback.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140307044201" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140307044201" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140307044201" decoding="async" width="180" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione blasting Greyback.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140307044201" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_blasting_Greyback.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione blasting <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, after he killed Lavender Brown during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Hermione demonstrated her exemplary abilities in <a href="/wiki/Martial_magic" title="Martial magic">martial magic</a> on numerous occasions, showing remarkable <a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">duelling</a> skill for her age. She can magically manipulate objects around herself to incapacitate or evade others.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPf_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPf-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> She had very fast reflexes when it came to wand work; for instance, she drew her wand and placed a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> between Harry and Ron when they were quarrelling before either of them could even draw their wands in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, and when the trio was spotted by Death Eaters during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, she was the first to react, sending them to safety.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Her duelling style was creative and unpredictable, mixing non-combat spells along with more conventional combative spells to overcome her opponents. Although she was incapacitated relatively early in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, Hermione removed two <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> from the fight in that short time.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> By the time she accompanied Ron and Harry on the search for the Horcruxes, her spell-work was swifter than opponents such as <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>: Hermione defeated <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">blasted</a> <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> to defend Harry, repelled <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a> when he forcibly <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Disapparated</a> with her, blasted <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> away from an injured <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, and saved him and Ron from being apprehended by Death Eaters when the trio went to see <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a>. She defeated many Death Eaters during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and held her own against <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> with the assistance of <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>. They weren't able to defeat her, but this likely because Hermione was fighting at a great disadvantage: she was forced to fight Bellatrix with Bellatrix's own wand, that was still loyal to Bellatrix. Being able to hold her own in such a disadvantageous condition against a very powerful witch like Bellatrix was an exceptional feat, further proof of her duelling ability.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>We just need to wipe their memories. It’s better like that, it’ll throw them off the scent. If we killed them, it’d be obvious we were here.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ronald Weasley</b>: "<i>You’re the boss. But I’ve never done a Memory Charm.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Nor have I, but I know the theory. Obliviate.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione's talent for advanced charms<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>

<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 181px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140605151006" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="179" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Hermione Incendio Slytherin&#39;s Locket.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin&#39;s_Locket.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/179?cb=20140605151006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140605151006" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/179?cb=20140605151006" decoding="async" width="179" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Hermione Incendio Slytherin&#39;s Locket.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin&#39;s_Locket.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/70/DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/179?cb=20140605151006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Hermione_Incendio_Slytherin%27s_Locket.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione Granger using the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a> in an attempt to destroy the Sytherin Locket</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Hermione was exceptionally talented with charm-work and some of her most impressive magical feats were charms. In her first year, she effortlessly mastered the <a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Levitation Charm</a> in Charms class, and also quickly learnt how to cast other charms such as the <a href="/wiki/Unlocking_Charm" title="Unlocking Charm">Unlocking Charm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Flashing_paint_charm" title="Flashing paint charm">Flashing paint charm</a> without difficulty.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> She not only achieved an '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> but also received a hundred and twelve percent in her first year Charms exam.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Hermoine enchanted her <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_handbag" class="mw-redirect" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s handbag">small handbag</a> with an <a href="/wiki/Extension_Charm" title="Extension Charm">Undetectable Extension Charm</a> to allow her to carry more items in the bag than physically allowed, which allowed her, Harry and Ron to survive the months spent out in the open. She managed to cast the <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">Memory Charm</a> successfully multiple times after having only read the theory behind it,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> affecting <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> even when they were subjected to the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Mione_obliate.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20160809012441" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mione obliate.JPG" data-image-key="Mione_obliate.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Mione_obliate.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160809012441" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Mione_obliate.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20160809012441" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Mione_obliate.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160809012441" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mione obliate.JPG" data-image-key="Mione_obliate.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/15/Mione_obliate.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160809012441" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mione_obliate.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione erasing <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>'s memories</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> During her sixth year, she successfully cast the <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> on Cormac McLaggen. Her array of <a href="/wiki/Protego_totalum" title="Protego totalum">protective charms</a> she casted outside their defended her, Harry, and Ron for almost a year while they were searching for Voldemort's Horcruxes, while several far more experienced wizards were captured within months. Hermione's speciality was creating <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">portable, waterproof fires</a>. In her first year, she kept these fires in a jar, used them to distract Severus Snape, whom she thought was jinxing Harry's broom during his first Quidditch match, and to attack the <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a> when she, Harry, and Ron searched for the Philosopher's Stone. In her second year, she used her flames in Moaning Myrtle's bathroom to light the cauldron above one of the toilets while Polyjuice Potion was brewed so that Harry and Ron could interrogate Draco Malfoy about the Heir of Slytherin. During the <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux hunt</a>, she kept the flames in a jar to keep the trio warm during winter. However, the one charm she had trouble with was the Patronus Charm, something Harry noted when she tried casting it when he, she and Ron infiltrated the Ministry of Magic, perhaps indicating she lacked the self-confidence. That said, she learned how to cast the corporeal Patronus Charm in her <a href="/wiki/1995-1996_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1995-1996 school year">fifth year</a> and was the first to master the advanced spell in Dumbledore's Army under Harry's tutelage, hers taking the form of an otter.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She mentioned in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> that she had been practising how to use her Patronus for messaging,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> but it is unknown if she ever actually carried this out.</li></ul>

<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Hermione was particularly talented in transfiguration. She was the first in her class to succeed at transfiguring a <a href="/wiki/Match_to_needle_spell" title="Match to needle spell">match into a needle</a> in their first lesson, long before any other student.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In 1994, she was the only one able to transform a <a href="/wiki/Hedgehog_to_pincushion_spell" title="Hedgehog to pincushion spell">Hedgehog to a pincushion</a>. Hermione earned an '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>' in her <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> exam, learning to <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">vanish</a> objects, one of its hardest spells. In 1995, she was able to vanish Harry Potter's <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potion</a> after believing him to be finished with it and a kitten by mid-year - the hardest vanishment challenge of all. Hermione was very skilled at <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjuration</a>, an advanced type of transfiguration. In her sixth year, she was able to conjure <a href="/wiki/Bird-Conjuring_Charm" title="Bird-Conjuring Charm">a flock of canaries</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> By the <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">next year</a>, she could conjure a <a href="/wiki/Orchideous" title="Orchideous">wreath of flowers</a> and a flask <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_magic" class="mw-redirect" title="Nonverbal magic">non-verbally</a>. Hermione could also perform <a href="/wiki/Human_Transfiguration" title="Human Transfiguration">Human Transfiguration</a>, which is noted to be very difficult and did so in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> to disguise Ron during the <a href="/wiki/1998_Break-in_of_Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" class="mw-redirect" title="1998 Break-in of Gringotts Wizarding Bank">break-in at Gringotts Bank</a>. She could also cast various other transfiguration spells, such as the <a href="/wiki/Lapifors_Spell" title="Lapifors Spell">Lapifors Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Draconifors_Spell" title="Draconifors Spell">Draconifors Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Snufflifors_Spell" title="Snufflifors Spell">Snufflifors Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avifors_Spell" title="Avifors Spell">Avifors Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ducklifors_Jinx" title="Ducklifors Jinx">Ducklifors Jinx</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pullus_Jinx" title="Pullus Jinx">Pullus Jinx</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Vermiculus_Jinx" title="Vermiculus Jinx">Vermiculus Jinx</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POAG_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAG-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GOFG_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFG-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007222911" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PetrificusTotalus PS.gif" data-image-key="PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007222911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007222911" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007222911" decoding="async" width="180" height="80" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PetrificusTotalus PS.gif" data-image-key="PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161007222911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione freezing <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Hermione was skilled in this subject as she was able to achieve an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' in her O.W.L.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In their first year, she mastered the <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In their third year when she took Professor Lupin's exam, Harry saw that she did everything perfectly except for the part of fighting the <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Despite this aptitude, this was the one subject Harry was better than her at, something she freely acknowledged.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hermione mastered all the spells taught by Harry in their fifth year in Dumbledore's Army. She mastered the <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a>, and various other offensive and defensive spells.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She was capable of using powerful defensive and offensive spells such as the <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">Blasting Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> If Hermione had become an Auror she would have excelled, but she instead dedicated herself to rebuilding the wizard laws. Alongside this, in one alternative universe created by Scorpius and Albus' time-travelling experiences, she became the professor of Defence Against the Dark Arts.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140306195438" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Blasting Curse DHF1.gif" data-image-key="Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140306195438" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140306195438" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140306195438" decoding="async" width="160" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Blasting Curse DHF1.gif" data-image-key="Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140306195438" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Blasting_Curse_DHF1.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione casting the Blasting Curse at Nagini in 1997</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Hermione was not known for her ability to perform dark magic and the extent of her capacity is truly unknown, but it could be assumed given her borderline genius status that she was no slouch, as she was able to successfully cast various potent <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a>. She was able to cast the <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a> and <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> in her first year,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Jelly-Legs_Jinx" class="mw-redirect" title="Jelly-Legs Jinx">Jelly-Legs Jinx</a> in her sixth,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and successfully cast a <a href="/wiki/Stinging_Jinx" title="Stinging Jinx">Stinging Hex</a> at a moment's notice.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hermoine had enough skill to come up with a very sophisticated <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinx</a> <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">that would deform the face of a person who betrayed the D.A</a>., which she taught to her comrades.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She also cast the <a href="/wiki/Oppugno_Jinx" title="Oppugno Jinx">Oppugno Jinx</a> to send several conjured canaries at Ron Weasley in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, to express her annoyance and anger at him for kissing Lavender Brown.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, she was able to cast a particularly powerful and destructive <a href="/wiki/Blasting_Curse" title="Blasting Curse">Blasting Curse</a>, which she used to blast Nagini with in Godric's Hollow in <a href="/wiki/December" title="December">December</a> <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>; a cast so powerful that it broke Harry's <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_wand" title="Harry Potter&#39;s wand">wand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20090706235941" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione during Potion class pic2.JPG" data-image-key="Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20090706235941" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20090706235941" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20090706235941" decoding="async" width="160" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione during Potion class pic2.JPG" data-image-key="Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20090706235941" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_during_Potion_class_pic2.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione attending <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a> in her sixth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Hermione was exceptionally gifted in the field of potion-making. She was able to identify <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potions</a> and their effects quickly after having only read about them.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> She was able to brew the very advanced and difficult Polyjuice Potion in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">second year</a> for her, Harry, and Ron to find the truth about the Chamber of Secrets from Draco Malfoy by disguising themselves as his friends.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> She achieved an 'Outstanding' on her Potions <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> and was only one of twelve to advance to N.E.W.T.-level. Hermione was the only one in her sixth year class who understood <a href="/wiki/Golpalott%27s_Third_Law" title="Golpalott&#39;s Third Law">Golpalott's Third Law</a>, without need for further explanation and was able to compose an antidote containing fifty-two ingredients, including a chunk of her own hair. The only time she was ever out-smarted in potions was in her sixth year by Harry Potter because he was using the <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Half-Blood Prince's old copy</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Advanced Potion-Making">Advanced Potion-Making</a> textbook that was full of hints and scribbles that helped Harry excel. This frustrated her greatly.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Hermione_Herbology.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190519155915" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Herbology.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Herbology.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Hermione_Herbology.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20190519155915" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Hermione_Herbology.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190519155915" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Hermione_Herbology.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20190519155915" decoding="async" width="150" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Herbology.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Herbology.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Hermione_Herbology.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20190519155915" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Herbology.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione Granger handling a Mandrake in a second year Herbology class</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a></b>: Hermione earned an 'Outstanding' O.W.L. in this subject, showing great talent in this field, and even studied it at N.E.W.T. level. She was particularly skilled in spells related to handling magical plants. In her first year, she saved Harry and Ron from some <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Underground_Chambers" title="Underground Chambers">Underground Chambers</a> by conjuring <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">Bluebell Flames</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> She had knowledge of various different plants; for example, in her <a href="/wiki/Second_year" title="Second year">second year</a>, she was the only one who knew what the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake" title="Mandrake">Mandrake</a> root was and of its potent <a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">healing</a> and restorative properties.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> She was also very capable of casting the <a href="/wiki/Herbivicus_Charm" title="Herbivicus Charm">Herbivicus Charm</a> by her fourth year, in order to magically growth plants at an excelled rate.<sup id="cite_ref-GOFG_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFG-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: Hermione had read a book containing information on Alchemy and the Philosopher's Stone in her first year.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> In her sixth year, she easily understood Golpalott's Third Law, meaning she had impressive knowledge of this very esoteric and mysterious branch of magic.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Hermione was the first in her <a href="/wiki/Apparition_(class)" title="Apparition (class)">class</a> to <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparate</a> successfully, achieving Apparition twice in that time and passed her test on the first attempt. According to Ron, her performance was "<i>perfect</i>" and the <a href="/wiki/Wilkie_Twycross" title="Wilkie Twycross">instructor</a> praised her talent greatly.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> While on the hunt for the Horcruxes with Harry and Ron, Hermione frequently Apparated and Disapparated the three of them using side-along Apparition, twice when they were falling through the air.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Arithmancy" title="Arithmancy">Arithmancy</a></b>: This was Hermione's favourite subject at Hogwarts. Considering she was one of the few people to take this subject, so she must have had considerable skill and knowledge in this field. She earned an 'Outstanding' O.W.L and took the subject to <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level, showing to have been exceptionally gifted in this field, given how Arithmancy is considered to be immensely difficult and complicated.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Dittany.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818235600" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="84" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dittany.gif" data-image-key="Dittany.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Dittany.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140818235600" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Dittany.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818235600" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Dittany.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140818235600" decoding="async" width="180" height="84" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dittany.gif" data-image-key="Dittany.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/Dittany.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140818235600" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dittany.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione healing a <a href="/wiki/Splinching" title="Splinching">Splinched</a> Ron with Dittany in 1997</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">Healing magic</a></b>: Hermione had impressive skills in and knowledge of healing magic. She had knowledge of the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake" title="Mandrake">Mandrake</a>'s healing properties in her second year,<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> and was able to skilfully take care of both Harry Potter's wound from fighting Nagini and Ron Weasley's splinching wound in 1997, using the medicinal plant <a href="/wiki/Dittany" title="Dittany">Dittany</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a></b>: Hermione was gifted in translating ancient runes into English. She earned an 'Outstanding' O.W.L. in the subject and took it to <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> This is what later helped lead her, Harry, and Ron to the Deathly Hallows. She later translated the original copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i> into English, which she published sometime before working at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a></b>: Hermione was very interested in the history of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> from a young age. Even before starting at Hogwarts, she bought several books and learned them by heart. She was one of very few students who payed attention to Professor Binns' lectures, being known to take excellent notes in the class. She earned an 'Outstanding' O.W.L. in the subject, which was hard to do,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> considering how boring the class was said to be.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a></b>: Hermione was known to have gained an 'Outstanding' O.W.L. in this subject, but she decided not to continue with it at N.E.W.T.-level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> She often helped Harry and Ron do their homework as they often didn't remember the required facts.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a></b>: This was one of the subjects Hermione chose to take in her third year with the aid of a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a>. She was exceptionally good at it because she could bring another point of view to the classroom and the lessons, achieving a score of over 300% on her final exam in third year. However, Hermoine dropped the subject after a year, as she was a Muggle-born witch and so knew a great deal about Muggles already.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a></b>: Hermione earned an 'Outstanding' O.W.L. in Care of Magical Creatures.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> She had no problem interacting with the <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">Hippogriff</a> <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> in her third year,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> but stated in her sixth that he scared her.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Her skills at interacting were demonstrated with her views on house-elves and her work on S.P.E.W.,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> having a good relationship with house-elves like Dobby and Winky and encouraging Harry to treat <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a> more kindly after he inherited him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> These skills allowed her to join the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_the_Regulation_and_Control_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures">Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures</a> where she continued her work with S.P.E.W., working for the rights of both house-elves and other underprivileged non-humans.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Although Hermione was not particularly confident with flying a <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a>, she was at least a reasonable flyer herself, as she was able to successfully fly on a broomstick in the <a href="/wiki/Underground_Chambers" title="Underground Chambers">Underground Chambers</a> in order to catch a <a href="/wiki/Winged_Keys" title="Winged Keys">Winged Key</a>, which she did without any difficulties, being able to soar through the air proficiently.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Spell_creation" title="Spell creation">Spell creation</a></b> (possibly): Hermione was highly implied to have successfully created at least one spell, a <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">jinx</a> that she placed upon the list of Dumbledore's Army members which, if activated, would cause the affected person's face to break out in boils that formed the word "SNEAK" and which could not be reversed by any known counter-spell. She may also have invented the Four-Point Spell, a useful spell that would make the user's wand point north to indicate direction. If so, this further shows her remarkable and outstanding skill and magical talent, as spell creation is noted to be extremely dangerous and only to be attempted by the most skilled wizards.</li>
<li><b>Intellectual giftedness</b>: Hermoine was noted to be a "<i>borderline genius</i>",<sup id="cite_ref-WBUR_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WBUR-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> getting top scores in every class, and getting 'Outstanding' in all her <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> except <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. She mentioned in her fifth year that the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> considered placing her in <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a>, but in the end decided on Sorting her into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hermione had a mastery of logic that most wizards lacked, as she stated that "<i>a lot of the greatest wizards haven't got an ounce of logic</i>". In 1992, she was able to use logic to get Harry past a protective measure that was taken to protect the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> by Severus Snape. Hermoine often provided the trio with vital information when carrying out research into the various mysteries they faced. For example, she was the one to figure out through research that the monster in the Chamber of Secrets was a Basilisk and in her third year that Professor Lupin was a werewolf. However, she tended to rely more heavily on facts and information that could be proven by background analysis rather than making intuitive leaps, so Harry was generally the one to put the pieces together which explain recent events to create the final picture and willing to make assumptions where Hermione disproved ideas if there was no clear evidence for them.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: While Harry did the majority of leading among the trio, it was usually Hermione who kept him on track when he, Ron and herself had a task to do, and she sometimes did the same only with Ron. She also helped form and co-lead Dumbledore's Army alongside Harry. Her leadership skills were again demonstrated when she joined the Ministry, helping improve the rights of House Elves and other underprivileged magical creatures in the Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures, and then getting promoted to Deputy Head of the Department of Magical Law Enforcement, in which she helped eradicate the old laws which only favoured pure bloods. Despite not desiring high positions and only leading when she was forced to do so and when the time was right, she was eventually promoted to the post of Minister for Magic before 2019.</li></ul>
