<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602200406" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg" data-image-key="HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602200406" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602200406" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602200406" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg" data-image-key="HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602200406" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:HermioneGrangerWandNN8411.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione's first wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_wand" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s wand">Vinewood wand</a></b>: Hermione purchased a 10¾" <a href="/wiki/Vine" title="Vine">vine</a> wood <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_wand" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s wand">wand</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_heartstring" title="Dragon heartstring">dragon heartstring</a> core in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>. There is a pattern of vines the whole way up the wands handle. She used it until the spring of <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, when she, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> were captured by <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a>, who confiscated their wands. She subsequently used <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Bellatrix Lestrange&#39;s wand">wand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Bellatrix Lestrange&#39;s wand">Bellatrix Lestrange's wand</a></b>: In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, after the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>, Hermione lost her own wand while Ron <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarmed</a> <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Harry grabbed Bellatrix's <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Bellatrix Lestrange&#39;s wand">wand</a> as they left and Hermione subsequently used it, though it didn't work well for her, as she did not win its allegiance. Hermione used this wand at least until the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, when she fought Bellatrix with her own wand.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png/revision/latest?cb=20161128043609" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="155" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange first wand.png" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161128043609" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png/revision/latest?cb=20161128043609" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161128043609" decoding="async" width="150" height="155" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange first wand.png" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161128043609" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_first_wand.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bellatrix Lestrange's first wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a></b>: In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, just before her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a> at Hogwarts, Hermione obtained a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> from the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> in order to facilitate her attending more classes. She also used it, at the end of the school year, to save <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Afterwards, Hermione returned the Time-Turner, returning to a normal class schedule.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_beaded_handbag" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s beaded handbag">Charmed handbag</a></b>: Hermione had a small, beaded <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_handbag" class="mw-redirect" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s handbag">handbag</a> on which she placed an <a href="/wiki/Extension_Charm" title="Extension Charm">Undetectable Extension Charm</a> in the summer of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>. She used the handbag to carry supplies such as clothing, books, <a href="/wiki/Dittany" title="Dittany">Dittany</a>, and camping equipment on her, Harry, and Ron's quest to locate and destroy Voldemort's Horcruxes. The bag was small enough to fit in her sock, so as to not have it stolen during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_coin" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army coin">Dumbledore's Army coin</a>:</b>: The Dumbledore's Army coin was a fake <a href="/wiki/Galleon" title="Galleon">Galleon</a> created by Hermione in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> to inform members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> when the next meeting would take place. She used it a great deal and ensured that her spellwork was good enough to disguise the information as typical text on a <a href="/wiki/Galleon" title="Galleon">Galleon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Revealer" title="Revealer">Revealer</a></b>: Hermione owned a <a href="/wiki/Revealer" title="Revealer">Revealer</a>, which renders invisible ink visible. She tried to use it on Tom Riddle's diary but no ink showed up.<sup id="cite_ref-COS13_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS13-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown if she still had it in her possession after 1992.</li>
<li><b>Spellbooks</b>: Hermione came to own various spellbooks for various <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">charms</a> that she learnt and studied throughout her Hogwarts education, for example the <a href="/wiki/Expelliarmus_spellbook" title="Expelliarmus spellbook">Expelliarmus spellbook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Glacius_spellbook" title="Glacius spellbook">Glacius spellbook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Reparo_spellbook" title="Reparo spellbook">Reparo spellbook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Draconifors_spellbook" title="Draconifors spellbook">Draconifors spellbook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Snufflifors_spellbook" title="Snufflifors spellbook">Snufflifors spellbook</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aqua_Eructo_spellbook" title="Aqua Eructo spellbook">Aqua Eructo spellbook</a> and <a href="/wiki/Herbivicus_spellbook" title="Herbivicus spellbook">Herbivicus spellbook</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> textbooks</b>: Whilst not a Dark witch, Hermione had an extensive knowledge of dark magic and owned various books on the subject, including <i><a href="/wiki/Magick_Moste_Evile" title="Magick Moste Evile">Magick Moste Evile</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Nightshade_Guide_to_Necromancy" title="The Nightshade Guide to Necromancy">The Nightshade Guide to Necromancy</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Dark_Arts" title="The Rise and Fall of the Dark Arts">The Rise and Fall of the Dark Arts</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Imperius_Curse_and_How_to_Abuse_It" title="The Imperius Curse and How to Abuse It">The Imperius Curse and How to Abuse It</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Sonnets_of_a_Sorcerer" title="Sonnets of a Sorcerer">Sonnets of a Sorcerer</a></i>, which could all be found on her bookshelf in her office in the Ministry. Additionally, during the Horcrux Hunt, Hermione kept a copy of <i>Secrets of the Darkest Art</i>, in which she learned of the dark magic that can be used to split one's soul and how the effects of having a split soul can affect the human being as a result of using such incredible and highly dark magic.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Magical_Theory" title="Magical Theory">Magical Theory</a></b>: Hermione owned a copy of this Hogwarts textbook on the theory of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>, which she usually kept stored in her school trunk. She would have used this extensively throughout her academic years, particularly in her <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Magical_Hieroglyphs_and_Logograms" title="Magical Hieroglyphs and Logograms">Magical Hieroglyphs and Logograms</a></b>: This book is about magical theory. Hermione used this reference book over breakfast one morning, in conjunction with a pile of other books, to work on her <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Ancient Runes</a> <a href="/wiki/Homework" title="Homework">homework</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Advanced_Rune_Translation" title="Advanced Rune Translation">Advanced Rune Translation</a></b>: Hermione owned a copy of this book, probably because it may have been required for her lessons in 6th year <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Ancient Runes</a> which she started in her third year with the aid of a time turner.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She was seen to be reading this book before the start of her sixth year, after her trip to <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ancient_Runes_Made_Easy" title="Ancient Runes Made Easy">Ancient Runes Made Easy</a></b>: The book was on a beginners' level for <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Ancient Runes</a> Hermione was seen reading it in her <a href="/wiki/Second_year" title="Second year">second year</a> when she was thinking about taking Ancient Runes for a subject in the following next year.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> She probably used the book in her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a> when she took the subject.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Spellman%27s_Syllabary" title="Spellman&#39;s Syllabary">Spellman's Syllabary</a></b>: Hermione owned a copy of this <a href="/wiki/Study_of_Ancient_Runes" title="Study of Ancient Runes">Study of Ancient Runes</a> which she would have used for her formal academic studies in the subject from her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a> onwards at Hogwarts.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Rune_Dictionary" title="Rune Dictionary">Rune Dictionary</a></b>: Hermione owned a Rune dictionary, which she consulted to help her understand and translate various complex ancient <a href="/wiki/Rune" title="Rune">runes</a> in her academic studies.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1f/Crookshanks3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114210529" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="175" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Crookshanks3.jpg" data-image-key="Crookshanks3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1f/Crookshanks3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20070114210529" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1f/Crookshanks3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114210529" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1f/Crookshanks3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20070114210529" decoding="async" width="150" height="175" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Crookshanks3.jpg" data-image-key="Crookshanks3.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1f/Crookshanks3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20070114210529" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Crookshanks3.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Crookshanks</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a></b>: Hermione obtained a ginger part-<a href="/wiki/Kneazle" title="Kneazle">Kneazle</a> cat <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>. Crookshanks is highly intelligent, but was not fond of many people besides Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown what happened to Crookshanks after Hermione left him at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> in the summer of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> in order to locate and destroy <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> It is very likely the two were reunited seeing their strong affection for one another.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png/revision/latest?cb=20161126064839" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="178" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tales of Beedle the Bard.png" data-image-key="Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161126064839" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png/revision/latest?cb=20161126064839" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161126064839" decoding="async" width="150" height="178" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tales of Beedle the Bard.png" data-image-key="Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6b/Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161126064839" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><i><b><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></b></i>: <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Will_and_Testament_of_Albus_Percival_Wulfric_Brian_Dumbledore" title="The Last Will and Testament of Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore">bequeathed</a> the original publication of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>, written in runes, to Hermione. It contained a clue about the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a> which led Hermione, Harry, and Ron to <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a>, who told them about the legendary items.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Later in life, Hermione translated the book into English and published her translation.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/An_Appraisal_of_Magical_Education_in_Europe" title="An Appraisal of Magical Education in Europe">An Appraisal of Magical Education in Europe</a></b>: This book is about <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_school" title="Wizarding school">wizarding schools</a> in <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>. Prior to <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Hermione had read it and learned of many things, including the <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a>'s reputation for having an emphasis on <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Magic</a>. It is also mentioned to have information about Beauxbatons Academy of Magic.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Later, in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Hermione considered taking this book with her as she was sorting supplies for their mission to find <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. It is not specified if it was one of the books she decided to bring with her when she left with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> It is, however, unlikely as it was of no real use to them on their mission.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Hogwarts_a_History.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111027025405" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="194" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hogwarts a History.jpg" data-image-key="Hogwarts_a_History.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Hogwarts_a_History.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20111027025405" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Hogwarts_a_History.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111027025405" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Hogwarts_a_History.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20111027025405" decoding="async" width="150" height="194" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hogwarts a History.jpg" data-image-key="Hogwarts_a_History.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/64/Hogwarts_a_History.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20111027025405" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hogwarts_a_History.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i>Hogwarts: A History</i> (Hermione's favourite book)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hogwarts:_A_History" title="Hogwarts: A History">Hogwarts: A History</a></b>: Hermione often referred to this book on many things concerning Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry. It was her favourite book and she would often read it in her free time. Three of the main topics brought up in it talk about Apparition within the castle,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Muggle electronics and the ceiling in the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore">The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore</a></b>: Hermione Granger had a copy of this book in her possession after her visit with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> to <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a> and their run in with <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> disguised as <a href="/wiki/Bathilda_Bagshot" title="Bathilda Bagshot">Bathilda Bagshot</a>. She picked it up as the two left the house and she read it while running and camping during her <a href="/wiki/Seventh_year" title="Seventh year">seventh year</a> with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, attempting to find clues which would help her and her friends locate and destroy <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Given her animosity towards the author, Rita Skeeter, it is highly unlikely that she kept it following the Second Wizarding War.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200420191232" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore - Mina Lima cover.jpg" data-image-key="The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20200420191232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200420191232" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20200420191232" decoding="async" width="150" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Life and Lies of Albus Dumbledore - Mina Lima cover.jpg" data-image-key="The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20200420191232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Life_and_Lies_of_Albus_Dumbledore_-_Mina_Lima_cover.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i>The Life and Lies of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Great_Wizarding_Events_of_the_Twentieth_Century" title="Great Wizarding Events of the Twentieth Century">Great Wizarding Events of the Twentieth Century</a></b>: This books is about prominent events in the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> during the twentieth century. <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> was mentioned in this book, which Hermione read before meeting him in person in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><b><a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Through_the_Ages" title="Quidditch Through the Ages">Quidditch Through the Ages</a></b></i>: Although she was not very interested in it, Hermione had read this book in her first year, which gave her some theoretical knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> and Quidditch balls. She knew about the Snitches' flesh memories, something of which Quidditch players Harry Potter and Ronald Weasley did not.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/The_Standard_Book_of_Spells,_Grade_4" title="The Standard Book of Spells, Grade 4">The Standard Book of Spells, Grade 4</a></b>: Hermione owned a copy of this popular Hogwarts textbook, which gave her the knowledge to study and learn various spells and charms for her <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a> of magical education at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart%27s_card_to_Hermione_Granger" title="Gilderoy Lockhart&#39;s card to Hermione Granger">Gilderoy Lockhart's card to Hermione Granger</a></b>: This letter was written by <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a> to Hermione in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, expressing his get-well wishes. Hermione hid it under her pillow in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> until her friends <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> discovered it.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_pencil_case" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s pencil case">Pencil case</a></b>: She had a large pencil case which allowed her to keep all her quill and other writing equipment together. She is first noted to have had it in her <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth year</a> when an argument with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> made her wipe her wet eyes on it.&lt;refname="HBP"/&gt; It is, however, highly possible that she owned this object since her <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a> and had not replaced it since.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110130060220" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="197" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Hermione Granger red dress robes full body shot.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110130060220" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110130060220" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110130060220" decoding="async" width="150" height="197" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Hermione Granger red dress robes full body shot.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110130060220" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Hermione_Granger_red_dress_robes_full_body_shot.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione in her dress robes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Spellotape" title="Spellotape">Spellotape</a></b>: Hermione Granger owned this popular brand of wizarding adhesive tape, which she once used to restrain a rogue biting copy of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Monster_Book_of_Monsters" title="The Monster Book of Monsters">The Monster Book of Monsters</a></i> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_dress_robes" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s dress robes">Dress robes</a></b>: Hermione wore a set of dress robes to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. They were made of a "<i>floaty, periwinkle-blue material</i>" and were considered to be quite attractive. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Hermione, once again, wore dress robes to the Wedding of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">William Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>. They were lilac in colour and had matching shoes.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_necklace" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s necklace">Red-jewel necklace</a></b>: This necklace was worn by Hermione to the wedding of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>. She wore it up until she ran away from the wedding after it was attacked by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. It was later destroyed by <a href="/wiki/Scabior" title="Scabior">Scabior</a> when she, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> were taken to <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Earrings.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120927193241" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Earrings.jpg" data-image-key="Earrings.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Earrings.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20120927193241" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Earrings.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120927193241" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Earrings.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20120927193241" decoding="async" width="150" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Earrings.jpg" data-image-key="Earrings.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Earrings.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20120927193241" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Earrings.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione's <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> earrings</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_scarf" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s scarf">A scarf</a></b>: Hermione owned a dark purple/red scarf and wore it frequently in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> whilst on the run with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> during the Second Wizarding War. She left it behind on their travels during her <a href="/wiki/Seventh_year" title="Seventh year">seventh year</a> and it was later picked up by Scabior.<sup id="cite_ref-DHF1_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHF1-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_Yule_Ball_earrings" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s Yule Ball earrings">Yule Ball earrings</a></b>: These were worn by Hermione to the Yule Ball in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>; her <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a>, which she attended with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, one of the four Champions in the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOFF_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFF-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_watch" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s watch">A watch</a></b>: This watch was worn and used by Hermione in her youth at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She was seen to be wearing it during her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Prefect_badge" title="Prefect badge">Prefect badge</a></b>: Having became a Hogwarts <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a> in her <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a>, she owned a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> Prefect badge, which she would have worn during her formal Prefect duties.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Glamchops" title="Glamchops">Glamchops</a> <a href="/wiki/Glamchops_Lemongrass_Hand_Lotion" title="Glamchops Lemongrass Hand Lotion">Lemongrass Hand Lotion</a> and <a href="/wiki/Glamchops_Moisturiser" title="Glamchops Moisturiser">Moisturiser</a></b>: Hermione Granger owned some bottles of these popular Muggle cosmetic products, which could be found in her bedroom.<sup id="cite_ref-DHF1_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHF1-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Omnioculars" title="Omnioculars">Omnioculars</a></b>: Hermione along with Ron were gifted a pair of these <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> <a href="/wiki/Binoculars" title="Binoculars">Binoculars</a> by Harry in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a> for the <a href="/wiki/1994_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="1994 Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a> that year.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Elf-Hat" title="Elf-Hat">Elf-Hat</a></b>: Hermione made several special hats which she hoped would be worn by <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">House elves</a> for the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>, which were unsuccessful. She later decided to wearing one herself when she went to visit <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> later that school year.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition_(class)" title="Apparition (class)">Licence to Apparate</a></b>: Hermione obtained her Licence to Apparate on April 21st, 1997.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> She passed her test flawlessly, according to Ron.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Parents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>I thought you were skiing with your mum and dad.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Well, to tell you the truth, skiing's not really my thing. So I've come for Christmas... Anyway, Mum and Dad are a bit disappointed, but I've told them that everyone who's serious about the exams is staying at Hogwarts to study. They want me to do well, they'll understand.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione telling <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> about changing her plans for the <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> <a href="/wiki/Christmas_holidays" title="Christmas holidays">Christmas holidays</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Hermione%27s_mother.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110623204724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="231" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s mother.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_mother.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Hermione%27s_mother.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110623204724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Hermione%27s_mother.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110623204724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Hermione%27s_mother.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110623204724" decoding="async" width="150" height="231" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s mother.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_mother.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Hermione%27s_mother.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110623204724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione%27s_mother.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_mother" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s mother">Mrs Granger</a>, her mother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Mr and Mrs Granger were <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Dentist" title="Dentist">dentists</a> who seemed proud of their <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a> daughter. They appeared to be accepting of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>, as they went shopping with Hermione in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> and allowed her to spend several holidays with the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> but did not approve of their daughter using magic as a quick-fix, as indicated by their not allowing Hermione to magically fix her teeth.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> They correspond by owl post with their daughter throughout the school year,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> but other than one holiday in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> with her parents, Hermione spent almost all of her time in the wizarding world. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, she planned to go <a href="/wiki/Skiing" title="Skiing">skiing</a> with them during the <a href="/wiki/Christmas_holidays" title="Christmas holidays">Christmas holidays</a>, but ended up going to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> to try to cheer Harry up instead. Hermione told her parents that the reason for her cancelling was to study for exams, indicating that her parents expected her to do well in school and were probably not aware of the extent of their daughter's involvement in activities relating to the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 147px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_father.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110623204413" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="145" height="239" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s father.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_father.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_father.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/145?cb=20110623204413" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_father.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110623204413" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_father.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/145?cb=20110623204413" decoding="async" width="145" height="239" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione&#39;s father.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione&#39;s_father.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Hermione%27s_father.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/145?cb=20110623204413" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione%27s_father.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger%27s_father" title="Hermione Granger&#39;s father">Mr Granger</a>, her father</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Assuming I survive our hunt for the Horcruxes, I'll find Mum and Dad and lift the enchantment. If I don't... well, I think I've cast a good enough charm to keep them safe and happy. Wendell and Monica Wilkins don't know that they've got a daughter, you see.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione on her parents' memory modification<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>To protect them during the height of the war, Hermione <a href="/wiki/False_Memory_Charm" class="mw-redirect" title="False Memory Charm">modified her parents' memories</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> to make them believe they were entirely different people, and they left the country.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> After the war, she found them in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> and restored their memories.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Children">Children</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Children">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Children"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>If you're not in Gryffindor, we'll disinherit you. But no pressure!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione and Ginny</b>: "<i>He doesn't mean it...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ginny reassuring Rose and Albus after Ron's joke<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Hermione_and_Rose.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111019230213" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione and Rose.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Rose.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Hermione_and_Rose.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111019230213" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Hermione_and_Rose.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111019230213" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Hermione_and_Rose.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111019230213" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione and Rose.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Rose.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Hermione_and_Rose.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111019230213" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_and_Rose.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione hugging Rose before Rose departs for <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">school</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Hermione had two children with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>: a daughter named <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and a son named <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a>.
</p><p>Rose started her first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, along with her cousin, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>. Ron stated that Rose had inherited her mother's brains. Hermione was probably very close to Rose because she was also described as smart, yet not a complete know-it-all.
</p><p>Hugo was born in <a href="/wiki/2006" title="2006">2006</a> or <a href="/wiki/2007" title="2007">2007</a>. He most likely inherited his father's <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> skills, as he was noted to fly a lot with his cousins <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Potter</a>. He also appeared to have a quiet demeanour.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nieces_and_nephews">Nieces and nephews</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 232px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206011704" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="230" height="161" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s kids.png" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_kids.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20141206011704" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206011704" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20141206011704" decoding="async" width="230" height="161" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s kids.png" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_kids.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/89/Harry%27s_kids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20141206011704" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%27s_kids.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Potter children, some of Hermione's nieces and nephews</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As four of <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>'s five surviving siblings were married by 2017, Hermione had quite a few nieces and nephews through her husband: <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> had three children (<a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily</a>), as did <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur</a> (<a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Weasley" title="Dominique Weasley">Dominique</a> and <a href="/wiki/Louis_Weasley" title="Louis Weasley">Louis</a>), while <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> and <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a> had a son and a daughter (<a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley_II" title="Fred Weasley II">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roxanne_Weasley" title="Roxanne Weasley">Roxanne</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> had two daughters (<a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley_II" title="Molly Weasley II">Molly</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lucy_Weasley" title="Lucy Weasley">Lucy</a>) with his wife, <a href="/wiki/Audrey_Weasley" title="Audrey Weasley">Audrey</a>. <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire Weasley</a>, one of Fleur and Bill's daughters, was seen kissing <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a> at <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Cross_Station" title="King&#39;s Cross Station">King's Cross Station</a>, by <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Potter</a>, Hermione's nephew and godson. Hermione visited them all on many occasions. It can be assumed that she was closest with Harry's children.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Weasley_family_members">Other Weasley family members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Other Weasley family members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Other Weasley family members"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>, her future in-laws</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Because of her friendships with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, Hermione became friendly with the entire <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>. She spent a portion of many of her summer holidays at their home of <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a>, and attended some family outings with them, such as shopping for school supplies in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> and attending the <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a> with them. <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> was fascinated by the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> world and thus Hermione's background, and even invited Hermione's <a href="/wiki/Granger_family" title="Granger family">parents</a> for a drink upon first meeting them. <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> was fond of Hermione, though she treated her coldly for a brief time after <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> printed lies about Hermione toying with the hearts of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, much to Hermione's bewilderment. After Harry explained that the stories were false, Mrs Weasley once again warmed up to Hermione. Also, she and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> were considered to be on good terms until their fight over elf rights.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>An Age Line! Well, that should be fooled by an Ageing Potion, shouldn’t it? And once your name’s in that goblet, you’re laughing — it can’t tell whether you’re seventeen or not!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>But I don’t think anyone under seventeen will stand a chance, we just haven’t learned enough . . .</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>Speak for yourself.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Fred disputing<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161120171013" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="176" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fred and George Weasley Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161120171013" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161120171013" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161120171013" decoding="async" width="235" height="176" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fred and George Weasley Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20161120171013" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fred_and_George_Weasley_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, her friends and future brothers-in-laws</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Fred and George Weasley seemed to regard Hermione and Harry almost like other younger siblings, teasing them as well as being protective of them. When <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> called Hermione a "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, the twins were outraged, and attempted to attack him.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Although Hermione disapproved of some of their antics, trying to use her status as a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> to keep them in line, she still got on well with them. Hermione once argued with them that the <a href="/wiki/Ageing_Potion" title="Ageing Potion">Ageing Potion</a> they planned on using to trick the age line protecting the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> wouldn't work because Dumbledore would have already thought of a foolish ageing potion. They didn't listen and tried to cross the line which resulted in them being thrown back and grow long, white beards.The only time she was notably angry with them was when they tested out their <a href="/wiki/Skiving_Snackbox" title="Skiving Snackbox">Skiving Snackboxes</a> on unsuspecting <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a> students; though the twins initially scoffed at her concerns and her ability to make them stop, they backed down when she threatened to tell their <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">mother</a>.
</p><p>However, Hermione still admired the cleverness and creativity of their spell work,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> once remarking that they could do some "<i>extraordinary magic</i>," which Fred was flattered enough by to offer Hermione material from their <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">joke shop</a> free of charge.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Fred and George also tried to get Hermione to relax, joking around with her about things such as their late uncle <a href="/wiki/Bilius" title="Bilius">Bilius</a>'s penchant for making mischief at weddings.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hermione was devastated when Fred was killed during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Hermione was not as close to the other Weasley siblings, though she was invited to <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> to <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>.
</p><p>With her marriage to Ron, Hermione became a part of the Weasley family herself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fleur_Delacour">Fleur Delacour</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119222230" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119222230" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119222230" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fleur_Delacour.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, her future sister-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Hermione first met Fleur Delacour, an incredibly beautiful, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a>, part-<a href="/wiki/Veela" title="Veela">Veela</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. Hermione disliked Fleur almost immediately, as she was given to fussily and loudly criticising nearly everything at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, from the weather, to the decoration and food. The fact that Ron had a little bit of a crush on Fleur didn't help, but he eventually got over it.
</p><p>Hermione, like Ginny and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Mrs Weasley</a>, was infuriated by Fleur's arrogance and constant complaining when <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> sent Fleur, his then fiancée, to <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> to get to know his family. However, when Fleur responded to Bill becoming permanently disfigured by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> with indignant denial that Bill's appearance would in any way effect their marital plans, Hermione most likely set her feelings aside.
</p><p>Despite seeming rather inconsiderate and self-centred, Fleur proved to be courageous and ultimately caring, even selfless, in her own way. She put her life in danger by posing as one of Harry's decoys in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, and after the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Battle of Malfoy Manor</a>, Hermione, Harry and Ron, along with <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, and an injured <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a>, stayed with Bill and Fleur for a month at <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>, where Fleur took care of them all like a mother. Later, Fleur became Hermione's sister-in-law through her marriage to <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a>, and Hermione's marriage to <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romances">Romances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Romances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Romances"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley">Ron Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;MuggleNet">"<i>Oh, maybe she and Ron will be alright with a bit of counselling, you know. I wonder what happens at wizard marriage counselling? They'll probably be fine. He needs to work on his self-esteem issues and she needs to work on being a little less critical.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> on Hermione and Ron's adult relationship<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/MuggleNet" title="MuggleNet">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101104210200" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101104210200" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/85/Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101104210200" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, the love of her life and father to her children</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ronald Weasley was, essentially, the love of Hermione's life. Although their relationship would have many ups and downs, Hermione and Ron Weasley were good friends for most of their years at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and of course, were best friends with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, who was usually a mediator in their disputes. They tended to argue frequently, though they usually got over their arguments, which tended to be minor or about trivial issues, although there were a few times when it seemed as if their friendship would be irreparable. As they grew older and matured, Ron and Hermione tended to fight less often and become more in touch with their feelings for each other. Hermione sometimes had the tendency of calling <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> "<i>Ronald</i>". Their first major falling-out was in their third year, when Ron accused Hermione's pet cat <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> of eating his pet rat <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hints of her feelings for Ron were shown as early as their first year, when she was badly hurt emotionally when he made fun of her for not having friends due to her bookish and bossy nature. According to Neville she spent the whole afternoon crying in the loo before the incident with the troll took place. In their third year Ron saw Sirius Black standing over him with a knife, Hermione was shocked and scared the most and even cried. They were both very awkward and embarrassed at times, being insecure with their own feelings for each other. Ron was used to always being in Harry's shadow and did not want the girl he loved to be also taken from him by his best friend. Hermione was greatly offended when Ron initially didn't ask her to the Yule Ball as his partner until he got rejected by Fleur Delacour. When it is revealed Viktor Krum was Hermione's date, a jealous Ron got into a heated row with Hermione, which she ended by making clear that she would go as Ron's date in future if only he asked her as his first choice. Ron and Hermione's relationship again suffered when Ron began dating <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, though the two reconciled after Ron was accidentally poisoned, leaving Hermione shaken. Ron's relationship with Lavender ended soon after, and both he and Hermione were more content for it.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 177px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160731041108" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="175" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20160731041108" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160731041108" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20160731041108" decoding="async" width="175" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/38/Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20160731041108" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron-y-Hermione-en-la-Madriguera.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron expressing their affection for each other</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Ron, you are the most insensitive wart I have ever had the misfortune to meet</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione tells Ron off for his insensitivity with girls' feelings<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Hints of romantic feelings between the two could be seen as early as their <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">second year</a>, as Ron was particularly protective of Hermione and disgusted by her crush on <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>.
