Also During the second year when Malfoy insulted Hermione calling her a mudblood an enranged Ron attempted to punish him with a curse, but as his wand was broken, the curse backfired on him injuring him.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Hermione was affronted by Ron's clumsy attempt to ask her to go with him, and Ron was jealous of her attendance with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>; this jealousy would persist for years. In turn, Hermione was jealous of Ron's crush on <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, though expressed it in a subtler way.
</p><p>In her fourth year while Harry and Ron were not in speaking terms following Harry's name coming out of the goblet of fire, Hermione defended Ron to Harry reminding him that despite him not wanting it he always gets all the attention while Ron had to live up competing with his five older brothers and Ron is always made to feel second to him.
</p><p>In their fifth year, Hermione kissed Ron on the cheek before the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Tournament</a>, to which he reacted by being "puzzled" and touching the spot where she kissed him. During Gryffindor's Quidditch try-outs in their sixth year, Hermione also <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confunded</a> Cormac McLaggen to increase Ron's chances of being made the team's Keeper. Also, Hermione became jealous (but she tried to conceal it) when Ron began dating <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a> and kissing her frequently.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110416015544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Ron and Hermione picking up stones.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20110416015544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110416015544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20110416015544" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Ron and Hermione picking up stones.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20110416015544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione spending time together during the Hocrux hunt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>I came running after you! I called you! I begged you to come back!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I know. Hermione, I'm sorry, I'm really—</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Oh, you're </i>sorry<i>! You came back after weeks — </i>weeks<i> — and you think it's all going to be all right if you just say sorry?... Weeks and weeks, we could have been </i>dead<i>…</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron after the latter's return to her and Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>By the summer of <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, the two were closer than ever and "sort of" together, according to Harry. They danced together at <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and Fleur's <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a>, and were generally kinder to one another. During the hunt for the <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, Ron comforted Hermione several times by putting his arm around her, and Harry believed that they might have fallen asleep holding hands. When Harry was briefly shouting at Hermione who was confronting him aboust his fallout with Remus Lupin and Harry was shouting at her, Ron defended Hermione from Harry by angrily saying "“Don’t you start on her!” Hermione was extremely upset when Ron temporarily left her and Harry, crying often, and she was absolutely furious with him when he returned. It was also revealed, through a vision caused by the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">locket Horcrux</a>, that one of Ron's deepest fears was that Hermione preferred Harry to him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140611234353" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="147" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron kissing in the Chamber of Secrets.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140611234353" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140611234353" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140611234353" decoding="async" width="240" height="147" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron kissing in the Chamber of Secrets.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140611234353" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione's first kiss during the Battle of Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two eventually made up, and Hermione initiated a kiss during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, when Ron suggested saving the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a> and not ordering them to fight for wizards. Hermione, who had been a promoter of house-elf rights since her fourth year and even started her own society to help house-elves (the <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare</a>) was so delighted at Ron's unexpected display of sensitivity that she kissed him on the lips, something that was met with surprise, eagerness and enthusiasm, but caused the pair to become embarrassed after Harry asked them to "<i>hold it in</i>".
</p><p>Some people had expected Ron and Hermione to become more than friends much sooner and Harry Potter had even thought that they would start dating in their sixth year. In the fifth year while Hermine and Harry were arguing about Harry's decision to talk to Sirius, Hermione asked Ron's advice in a manner that "reminded irresistibly of Mrs Weasley appealing to her husband during Harry’s first dinner in Grimmauld Place."  In 1997, when the Trio was captured by <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> and brought to <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> mistakenly called Ron Hermione's boyfriend when she tried to protect him. Also, Ron screamed and yelled and was in terrible distress when he heard Hermione being tortured by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> in Malfoy Manor. The pair eventually married and had two children, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo Weasley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They were rather young when they were married, and their relationship evolved over time. By the time that Hermione was elected Minister For Magic, Ron had become more the stay-at-home-dad due to the convenience it placed on their respective careers, as Ron's entrepreneurial exploits could be more easily conducted than Hermione's careers in law enforcement and eventually politics. Their combative relationship eventually subsided for a more affectionate one, as Ron was seen to kiss Hermione in public extremely often as noted by their nephew, Albus Potter. Hermione was initially wary when Ron spoke of how early they had married and was jokingly suspicious that he wanted a break from their marriage, but was deeply moved when Ron told her that he wanted to renew their vows and marry her all over again after reading about how Muggles occasionally did such a thing. Hermione was so touched by her husband's suggestion that they began to kiss passionately over her mountain of paperwork in her office. This shows how Ron had matured into a startling romantic over the years and how it helped to temper their initially rocky relationship that begun 31 years prior.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Viktor_Krum">Viktor Krum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Viktor Krum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Viktor Krum"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>How did <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">she</a> know Viktor asked me to visit him over the summer?... Madam Pomfrey gave us both blankets and then he sort of pulled me away from the judges so they wouldn't hear, and he said, if I wasn't doing anything over the summer, would I like to —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>And what did you say?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>And he did say he'd never felt the same way about anyone else...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione about Viktor Krum's invitation to spend the summer with him.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103135847" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="232" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-image-key="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141103135847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103135847" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141103135847" decoding="async" width="165" height="232" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-image-key="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141103135847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Goffilm39.1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, her friend and Yule Ball date</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Viktor Krum, a renowned professional <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player and student of <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang</a>, came to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, in which he was a Champion. He took to following Hermione into the library, watching her and trying to "<i>pluck up the courage</i>" to speak to her. Eventually, he asked her to be his date to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, and Hermione accepted. Their arrival together caused something of a stir, given Viktor's fame and Hermione's exceptional, and rather unexpected, beauty.
</p><p>Hermione was Viktor's 'hostage' during the Second Task of the Tournament. After he pulled her from the lake, Viktor told Hermione that he had never felt about someone the way he felt about her, and invited her to visit him in <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a> over the summer.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> At some point, it is alleged by Ginny Weasley during a confrontation with her brother Ron, that he and Hermione shared a kiss during that period.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Whether or not Ginny was just trying to get under Ron's skin or if this actually happened is unknown. What is known is that their relationship never became serious enough for her to visit him in Bulgaria, they kept in contact through letters over the years.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> They met again at the <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, where Viktor complimented Hermione and was disappointed to learn that she had "sort of" begun a romance with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends">Friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Friends">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Friends"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>[Harry] put his arm around Hermione's shoulders, and she put hers around his waist, and they turned in silence and walked away through the snow, past Dumbledore’s mother and sister, back toward the dark church and the out-of-sight kissing gate.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry and Hermione share a moment at his parents' grave<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 170px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="168" height="228" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180528175859" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" decoding="async" width="168" height="228" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter movies hbp promostills 6.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/168?cb=20180528175859" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_movies_hbp_promostills_6.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, her best friend and future co-brother-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione became friends with Harry Potter after they as well as <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> took down a <a href="/wiki/Mountain_Troll" class="mw-redirect" title="Mountain Troll">Mountain Troll</a> together in their first year.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> They tended to get along very well on a day-to-day basis, though Harry occasionally became annoyed by Hermione's nagging, while she occasionally became annoyed by his lack of discipline and conviction in his schoolwork. Their only notable row was over Hermione getting Harry's <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> confiscated in their third year, which she felt it might be a trap. Harry and Ron reconciled with Hermione after <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> scolded them for their treatment of her. Harry and Hermione were quite similar in their dour, brooding tendencies in times of trouble, and often needed Ron's humour and levity to counterbalance their intense personalities.
</p><p>Harry, Hermione, and Ron spent nearly all their time together during their years at Hogwarts, and shortly afterwards, Hermione led Harry through <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">time-travel</a>, and together they rescued <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>; Hermione breaking the rules of using her Time-Turner, something she admitted was incredibly dangerous, demonstrated the strength of her friendship with Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">following year</a>, Hermione was the only student who believed Harry when he told her he had not put his name in the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>, and spent much of the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> teaching Harry useful spells and trying to reconcile him and Ron.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Harry — you’re a great wizard, you know.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>I’m not as good as you.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Me! Books! And cleverness! There are more important things — friendship and bravery and — oh Harry — be careful!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione's bond with Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>While Harry and Hermione typically argued less than Ron and Hermione, they had the most philosophical and moral disagreements with one another. Ron typically deferred to Harry's opinions on important decisions, and tends to hold back when Hermione confronts Harry about them, letting them battle it out. For example, Harry and Hermione fought about how best to deal with <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> when she infiltrated Hogwarts, whether or not Sirius's judgement could be trusted, whether or not Harry should have tried to use <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> to block out his mental link with Voldemort, whether Dumbledore's past made him an unworthy leader, and whether they should have pursued the Hallows or the Horcruxes. Hermione expressed immense displeasure to Harry during the sixth year after he started obtaining better results than her at Potion by the help of the "Half Blood Prince's potions book". Harry tended to be dismissive of Hermione's opinions, and could even grow angry when she tried to argue her point, but many times realised later that she was right. For example, Harry was often dismissive of Hermione's insistence that all <a href="/wiki/House-elves" class="mw-redirect" title="House-elves">house-elves</a> deserve respect and kindness, and was neglectful towards <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a> because of his bigotry until he finally realised the horrifying nature of his enslavement.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif/revision/latest?cb=20150722165057" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="POA Hermione shielding Harry Shrieking Shack.gif" data-image-key="POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150722165057" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif/revision/latest?cb=20150722165057" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150722165057" decoding="async" width="240" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="POA Hermione shielding Harry Shrieking Shack.gif" data-image-key="POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150722165057" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:POA_Hermione_shielding_Harry_Shrieking_Shack.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione protecting Harry, demonstrating her willingness to put his best interests first</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Harry tended to have more fun with Ron, Hermione was consistently his place of refuge when others abandoned him, from Ron's jealous withdrawal during the Triwizard Tournament, to Harry's discovery of Dumbledore's past during the war. Despite their differences, Harry and Hermione tended to support one another at the expense of others when necessary. Hermione repeatedly chose to help and support Harry in his fight against Voldemort, regardless of personal cost. Examples include breaking the laws regarding time travel in order to help him save Sirius, teaching him defensive magic in preparation for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, blackmailing <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> in order to give him a way to tell the public about Voldemort's return, protecting him from torture by Dolores Umbridge, and Obliviating her parents in order to go on the run with him. She notably chose to support him even when Ron did not. Smaller acts of friendship included helping him with homework and cheering him on at Quidditch games.
</p><p>Harry was similarly protective and supportive of Hermione. Much like Hermione, Harry was often a place of refuge for Hermione when others leave her. Harry often comforts Hermione and shows her kindness and care when she is upset. On the occasion that Buckbeak the Hippogriff is executed, Harry consoles her as she cries.
</p><p>He was also quick to defend Hermione from Cho Chang, Draco Malfoy, and others who insulted her for her looks or parentage, which showed his pride in her intellect on numerous occasions. He consistently praised her intelligence and magical skills to teachers, asked her for help in dangerous situations, and defended her against bullies. On one occasion, he even choose to side with her over Ron when was dating Lavender. But he expressed outrage when Hermione went to Slughorn's party with Cormac McLaggen.
</p><p>Harry also defended Hermione physically on instinct. This showed his willingness to put her before himself as well as his unconditional brotherly love for her. For example, when Lupin turns into a werewolf and attacked Hermione and Harry in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Harry shielded her from the danger.
</p><p>Many people, including <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor, Krum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Mrs Weasley</a>,, have occasionally mistaken Harry and Hermione's relationship to be a romantic one, given their closeness and expressions of physical affection, such as kisses on the cheek, staying by one another's bedsides when hurt or injured, embracing each other, and holding hands.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Harry eventually explained to Ron that he and Hermione were like brother and sister.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> They shared similar upbringings as being only children raised in the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> world, and showed each other unconditional love despite their many differences and disagreements. During their time alone during the war, Ron and Harry maintained a distance with Hermione mostly crying for Ron and Harry observing Ginny's dot at the maruderer's map. They did exchange a comforting moment during their brief embrace after Harry visited his parent's grave.<sup id="cite_ref-HAH_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HAH-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hermione and Harry remained best friends into adulthood, and eventually became co-siblings in-law when Hermione married <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and Harry married <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. Hermione was also the aunt and godmother of Harry's three children: <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna</a>. They were also coworkers for many years as employees of the Ministry of Magic in law enforcement.
</p><p>It is interesting to note that Albus Dumbledore's final plan to defeat Lord Voldemort, in which Harry would learn the story of the Deathly Hallows in time to use them against Voldemort, revolved not only around Harry himself, but Hermione as well. Dumbledore knew that Harry was too passionate and angry to be able to keep from attempting to become Master of Death, and so entrusted <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i> to Hermione, so that she would learn of the Hallows' symbol first and would be able to caution and guide Harry down the path of reason.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ginny_Weasley">Ginny Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ginny Weasley </b>: "<i>Hermione told me to get on with life, maybe go out with some other people, relax a bit around you, because I never used to be able to talk if you were in the room, remember? And she thought you might take a bit more notice if I was a bit more — myself.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Smart girl, that Hermione.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny regarding how she confides in Hermione<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127043147" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20101127043147" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127043147" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20101127043147" decoding="async" width="160" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ginny Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Ginny_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Ginny_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20101127043147" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ginny_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, her good friend and future sister-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ginny Weasley was Hermione's best female friend and Ginny's confidante. The two grew close when Hermione stayed in Ginny's room at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> during her many summertime visits. Ginny was the only one Hermione told about being asked to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> by <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> while Hermione was the only one who knew that Ginny had been learning to fly in secret for years.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She also gave Ginny advice about dealing with her feelings for Harry — advice that eventually led to the two dating,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and eventually marrying.
</p><p>Hermione comforted Ginny after an encounter with <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> upset her in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and after the death of her brother <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> However, Hermione would not have been afraid to stand up to Ginny when she felt that Ginny was wrong. The two remained very close after <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">the war</a> and eventually became sisters-in-law when Hermione married Ron, making her an aunt to Ginny's three children, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily</a>, as well as being chosen to be godmother to Ginny's eldest son James, and making Ginny Rose and Hugo's aunt and almost certainly Rose's godmother.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Phineas Nigellus</b>: "<i>Exactly what claim did the Weasley girl have upon it? She deserved her punishment, as did the idiot Longbottom and the Lovegood oddity!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Neville is not an idiot and Luna is not an oddity!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The portrait of <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> discussing the attempted theft of <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Gryffindor's Sword</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="154" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140610141612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140610141612" decoding="async" width="154" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20140610141612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, her friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was good friends with Neville Longbottom. They met on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">train</a> to Hogwarts during their first year and she helped him search for his toad <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Hermione helped Neville many times with their school work, particularly with <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> noted that she was often "<i>hissing instructions in his ear</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> In their <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">fourth year</a>, Hermione noticed Neville's horrified reaction to witnessing the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> be performed on a <a href="/wiki/Spider" title="Spider">spider</a> by Professor <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> (actually <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>), and shrieked for the teacher to stop. That same year, Neville asked Hermione to attend the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with him, as she had "<i>always been really nice</i>" to him, though she had already agreed to accompany <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hermione often fiercely defended Neville when others insulted him, and her friendship and support, as well as that of other <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> members, likely contributed to Neville gradually gaining self-confidence and courage.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Neville was obviously very fond of Hermione, and appreciative of her kindness and all the help she had given him. It was hinted that he spoke of her frequently to his grandmother, <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>, who seemed to already know a good deal about Hermione when they first met at Saint Mungo's in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. Following the war, they kept in touch.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Luna_Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>What about Luna?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Well, if they're telling the truth and she's still alive —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Don't say that, don't say it! She must be alive, she must!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione, Ron, and Harry after their escape from the <a href="/wiki/Lovegood_House" title="Lovegood House">Lovegood House</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220801" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luna Lovegood profile Deathly Hallows.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220801" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220801" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220801" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luna Lovegood profile Deathly Hallows.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/22/Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220801" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luna_Lovegood_profile_Deathly_Hallows.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, a good friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although Hermione rarely saw eye-to-eye with Luna Lovegood due to their very different world views and beliefs, the two became very good friends through <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. Hermione first met Luna on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>; she insulted <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i>, but backtracked when Luna told her that her <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">father</a> was the editor. Hermione was frustrated with Luna's belief in all manner of things without proof or logical grounds, but eventually simply accepted their differences, telling Luna that her planned trip to Sweden in search of a <a href="/wiki/Crumple-Horned_Snorkack" title="Crumple-Horned Snorkack">Crumple-Horned Snorkack</a> sounded "<i>lovely</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The following year, Luna comforted Hermione when she was upset over her fight with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Hermione was one of the five portraits Luna painted — along with Harry, Ron, Ginny, and Neville — and hung from her bedroom ceiling, the word "<i>friends</i>" linking them in gold writing. When <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a> attempted to turn Harry, Ron, and Hermione over to <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in exchange for his daughter's safety, Hermione <a href="/wiki/Ambush_at_the_Lovegood_House" title="Ambush at the Lovegood House">engineered their escape</a> so that the Death Eaters saw Harry briefly, thus ensuring that both Luna and her father were not harmed. Despite disagreeing with Luna on many things herself, Hermione defended her when others insulted her; for example, she tried to kick Ron for teasing Luna about <a href="/wiki/Gurdyroot" title="Gurdyroot">Gurdyroots</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, and snapped at the portrait of <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> for calling Luna an oddity. The two girls remained close friends in adulthood and saw each other regularly. Luna may be one of the best female friends of Hermione (along with Ginny), as she was only seen with these girls during her school-time at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black">Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>But Harry, you've just said it. <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> wanted you to learn to shut these things out of your mind, if you'd done <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> properly you'd never seen this —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>IF YOU THINK I'M JUST GOING TO ACT LIKE I HAVEN'T SEEN —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Sirius told you there was nothing more important than you learning to close your mind</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>WELL, I EXPECT HE'D SAY SOMETHING DIFFERENT IF HE KNEW WHAT I'D JUST —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and Hermione on Sirius Black being tortured<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150918055024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150918055024" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150918055024" decoding="async" width="165" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo front closeup Sirius Black.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20150918055024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_front_closeup_Sirius_Black.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, her friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione first learned about Sirius Black in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when he escaped <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. The wizarding world at large knew of him as the wizard who murdered twelve Muggles and a wizard (<a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>) with a single curse. Very few knew of his affiliation with the Potters and those who did also believed that Sirius had betrayed <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> to Voldemort by revealing their location at <a href="/wiki/Godric%27s_Hollow" title="Godric&#39;s Hollow">Godric's Hollow</a>. During the events at Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Hermione along with Harry, Ron and Lupin discovered that, contrary to their previous beliefs, Sirius Black had never committed the murders for which he had been incarcerated, nor had he betrayed his closest friends. 
</p><p>The trio managed to save Sirius and Lupin from being subjected to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> by firing three simultaneous <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charms</a> at him. Snape was blasted off his feet and knocked unconscious, allowing Harry, Ron and Hermione to continue their interrogation of Sirius who later revealed that Pettigrew had disguised himself in his rat <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> form for twelve years in order to escape justice and the wrath of Voldemort's remaining Death Eaters. However, upon exiting the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>'s secret passageway together, Pettigrew shrewdly used Lupin's werewolf transformation as a distraction and escaped. Sirius was soon apprehended and locked in <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>'s office to await the Dementor's Kiss. Harry and Hermione would later use the latter's <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to <a href="/wiki/Rescue_of_Sirius_Black_and_Buckbeak" title="Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak">rescue</a> Sirius, who became deeply grateful to both of them.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Hermione, Harry, and Ron visited Sirius at the cave off <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> village he was hiding in, bringing him food. Here they discussed the many mysteries that had occurred during that year, the trio learning valuable pieces of information regarding the imprisonment of <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> After the events of the Third Task, Sirius (while in his Animagus form) joined Hermione, Ron and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> at Harry's bedside, each indicating their affections for the latter.
</p><p>Hermione and Sirius would not meet again until the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, at the Headquarters of the second <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Sirius was obliged to remain in <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> for his own safety (his innocence not yet recognised by the Ministry). Sirius was rather disappointed when Harry was allowed to return to Hogwarts, Hermione pointing out that he had probably been secretly wishing that Harry had been expelled from school so that they could both stay at Grimmauld Place and be "<i>outcasts together</i>". Hermione expressed an even deeper understanding of Sirius's emotions when she stated her opinion to Harry that Sirius was attempting to relive his happier school days through his godson. Harry ignored this and became slightly agitated at the suggestion that Sirius might be guilty of such a crude, selfish mentality. However, she severely disapproved of his indifferent and occasionally cruel treatment of his <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a>, despite the fact that Kreacher initially appeared to be disgusted by her and addressed her as "the <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" (which Hermione often attributed to Kreacher being senile due to his old age.) 
</p><p>She also thought that Sirius was attempting to live vicariously through her, Harry and Ron when he encouraged them to form Dumbledore's Army, but the two boys became angry and snapped at her when she expressed this belief. Sirius was eventually killed by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, much to the dismay of his friends and loved ones. Hermione was devastated by his death, and often tried to provide comfort to Harry, who had been even more deeply affected by the tragedy. At the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Hermione became godmother to Harry's eldest son, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>, whose first and middle name was derived from James Potter and Sirius Black respectively.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Crookshanks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Crookshanks"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Hermione, that thing nearly scalped me!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>He didn't mean to, did you, Crookshanks?... Poor Crookshanks, that witch said he'd been in there for ages; no one wanted him.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I wonder why.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron when she bought Crookshanks<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_poa.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128082208" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="246" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione poa.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_poa.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_poa.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190128082208" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_poa.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128082208" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_poa.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190128082208" decoding="async" width="180" height="246" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione poa.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_poa.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Hermione_poa.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190128082208" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_poa.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione with Crookshanks</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> was Hermione's large, bandy-legged, half-<a href="/wiki/Kneazle" title="Kneazle">Kneazle</a>, ginger-coloured pet cat since she bought him from the <a href="/wiki/Magical_Menagerie" title="Magical Menagerie">Magical Menagerie</a> in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>. She seemed to think he was gorgeous, although no one else had wanted to buy him when he was still being sold at the Menagerie. She was proud of his cleverness. The latter proved to be quite true during the <a href="/wiki/1993-1994_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1993-1994 school year">1993-1994 school year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Crookshanks recognised that Hermione had left him at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> before Bill and Fleur's <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> most likely had been left in care of Mrs Weasley or Ginny, but it is possible that they were reunited after the Second War given the deep care and affection they had for each other.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_Students">Hogwarts Students</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts Students">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Hogwarts Students"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Roommates">Roommates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=51" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Roommates">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Roommates"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I love you, Hermione.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Don't let Lavender hear you saying that.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>I won't. Or maybe I will... then she'll ditch me...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> talking<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110719012047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg" data-image-key="Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20110719012047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110719012047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20110719012047" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg" data-image-key="Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20110719012047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jessie-Cave-M1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, her roommate and romantic rival</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione's roommates at Hogwarts were fellow <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a> Lavender Brown and Parvati Patil as well as <a href="/wiki/Fay_Dunbar" title="Fay Dunbar">Fay Dunbar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fay_Dunbar%27s_friend" class="mw-redirect" title="Fay Dunbar&#39;s friend">another girl</a>. While Lavender and Parvati swiftly became best friends, Hermione was not very close to either of them. Although the girls did not dislike each other, they had very different interests and sometimes clashed as a result. 
</p><p>For example, Hermione scorned <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>, Lavender and Parvati's favourite subject, and accidentally upset Lavender with her clumsy attempt to comfort her over the death of her rabbit.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Hermione was also angry with Lavender for doubting <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s assertion that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> had returned in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> and snapped at her about it. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 161px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/ParvatiPoA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090223025821" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="159" height="224" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="ParvatiPoA.jpg" data-image-key="ParvatiPoA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/ParvatiPoA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20090223025821" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/ParvatiPoA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090223025821" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/ParvatiPoA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20090223025821" decoding="async" width="159" height="224" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="ParvatiPoA.jpg" data-image-key="ParvatiPoA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/ParvatiPoA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20090223025821" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:ParvatiPoA.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati Patil</a>, her roommate</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Lavender began dating Ron Weasley, she was very upset and confided in Harry about her feelings. Once they broke up however, Hermione chose to not display open affection towards Ron so Lavender's feelings would not get hurt. She also came to Lavender's rescue during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, blasting <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> away from her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Unfortunately Lavender was mortally wounded by Greyback and was already dead by the time Hermione reached her. It can be assumed that Hermione was at least saddened by Lavenders death.
</p><p>Hermione had a less tumultuous relationship with Parvati, although the two were not close. During Hermione's first year at Hogwarts, she hugged Parvati after Harry caught the Snitch at a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> game. Parvati was noted to feel guilty after laughing at Ron's cruel teasing of Hermione in <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>, and the two discussed Hermione's attendance of the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Slug Club Christmas party</a> with <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>. As Parvati looked “<i>positively agog</i>” at Hermione confiding in her,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> it can be assumed that Hermione seldom discussed personal matters with her room mates.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Cormac_McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=52" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Cormac McLaggen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Cormac McLaggen"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>What's happened to you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Oh, I've just escaped — I mean, I've just left Cormac. Under the mistletoe... Cormac hasn't asked me one single question about myself, no, I've just been treated to 'A Hundred Great Saves Made by Cormac McLaggen' non-stop ever since — oh no, here he comes!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione avoiding her date<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 157px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110224235356" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="155" height="252" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mclaggen.jpg" data-image-key="Mclaggen.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20110224235356" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110224235356" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20110224235356" decoding="async" width="155" height="252" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mclaggen.jpg" data-image-key="Mclaggen.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20110224235356" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mclaggen.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Cormac McLaggen</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a> was a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> student one year above Hermione. The two became acquainted in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> through the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, of which they were both members, though Hermione did not think highly of McLaggen. When she overheard him insulting <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> during <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> try-outs, Hermione struck him with the <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a>, undermining his abilities as a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a>. 
</p><p>Later in the year, when Hermione was furious with Ron for dating <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, she decided to attend <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Christmas party</a> with McLaggen because she knew Ron despised him. McLaggen was apparently interested in Hermione, as he escorted her to the party and was very forward with her romantically while there. This, as well as his tendency to boast about himself, put Hermione off, and she soon abandoned him for the company of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a> before leaving the party altogether to avoid him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_23-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> It can be assumed that the party was the end of their interaction.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Cho_Chang.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180322164130" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Cho Chang.jpg" data-image-key="Cho_Chang.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Cho_Chang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180322164130" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Cho_Chang.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180322164130" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Cho_Chang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180322164130" decoding="async" width="180" height="263" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Cho Chang.jpg" data-image-key="Cho_Chang.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Cho_Chang.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180322164130" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cho_Chang.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Cho Chang in her fifth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Cho_Chang"><a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=53" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Cho Chang">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Cho Chang"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hermione had a two sided history with Cho; while Hermione offered <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> advice for making his relationship with Cho successful, Cho thought that Hermione’s friendship with Harry was romantic and got increasingly jealous of her since Harry spends so much time with her. Hermione has no grudges for Cho however and was not angry at her when Harry told Hermione that Cho insulted her, instead rather cross at Harry for messing up his own relationship. When Harry arrives at the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> with Ron and Hermione, shortly after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> all hard feelings seemed to have been forgotten or forgiven as Cho greeted Hermione in a friendly way, probably since Cho had long broke up with Harry. The two seemed to be on neutral terms.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=54" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Enemies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Enemies"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=55" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Harry, he has overpowered the Ministry, the newspapers, and half the wizarding community! Don't let him enter your mind, too!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione Granger regarding Voldemort<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140630194830" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="232" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle DHF2.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140630194830" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140630194830" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140630194830" decoding="async" width="166" height="232" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle DHF2.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20140630194830" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, her enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione first learned about Lord Voldemort, the most dangerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> of all time, after reading about him sometime before she began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. During her first year, she and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> helped <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> reach the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> and protect it from Voldemort. 
</p><p>A year later, Hermione, after fully recovering from her Polyjuice mishap, was shown <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">T. M. Riddle's Diary</a> by Harry. At first enthusiastic that the book might have "magical powers", Hermione first came up with the theory that it was Tom Riddle who originally "caught" the "Heir of Slytherin" when the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> had been opened fifty years prior.
