She also correctly guessed that the Diary contained the answers to the Chamber's location, how to open it, and the true identity of Slytherin's monster. Thinking that the Diary was written in invisible ink, the attempted to use the spell <i><a href="/wiki/Revealing_Charm" title="Revealing Charm">Aparecium</a></i>, and then a <a href="/wiki/Revealer" title="Revealer">Revealer</a>, on the object, but to no effect. Later on, when Harry went to the trophy room to try to learn more about Tom Riddle, he was accompanied by an "interested" Hermione. When Ron compared Riddle to Percy "in disgust", mentioning the former as being "<i>Prefect, Head Boy... probably at the top of every class</i>", Hermione responded in a "slightly hurt" voice, "<i>You say that like it's a bad thing</i>."  
</p><p>Later on, she also correctly deduced that Riddle had "caught the wrong person", and that "<i>it was some other monster</i> [not Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>] <i>that was killing people</i>". Later on, after Harry mentioned "hearing the voice" again before the Quidditch match between Gryffindor and Hufflepuff, Hermione ran immediately to the Library to research, where realised that Slytherin's monster was a basilisk. Tearing the page out of the book, and putting it in her right hand, she left the Library, where she warned the first person she met, Penelope Clearwater, to look around corners with her mirror. However, both Hermione and Penelope were petrified  by <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">Salazar Slytherin's Basilisk</a>, which was controlled by Tom Riddle's memory. 
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, she learned that the Dark Lord had returned and supported Harry against the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>'s denial and smear campaign. She also fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> to prevent Voldemort from obtaining a vital <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">prophecy</a>, but was severely injured and rendered unconscious. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, she left Hogwarts to help Harry and Ron find and destroy Voldemort's horcruxes. She personally destroyed <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Helga Hufflepuff's Cup</a> using a <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">basilisk</a>'s fang. She later witnessed Harry's defeat of Voldemort in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>However, Hermione made very little direct contact with Voldemort, truly seeing him for the first time during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. Possibly the closest connection Hermione and Voldemort shared was through the former wearing <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> whilst travelling with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> in 1997. The <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> locket was worn by all three for regular, though limited, periods of time, inadvertently allowing the portion of soul within to access the wearer's thoughts, emotions and deepest fears. The Horcrux had learned enough about Hermione to use hers and Harry's likenesses in emotionally torturing Ron, reflecting Ron's deepest fears of Hermione preferring Harry to him. Because the Horcrux had become so disconnected from the once whole soul of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a>, the physically bodied Voldemort was not aware of any of these events, nor of the information the Horcrux had gained dangling around the necks of Harry and his closest friends. 
</p><p>Although they had very little direct contact, Hermione and Voldemort are sometimes similar: both are "<i>model students</i>" who achieved outstanding grades in NEWTS. Both were Prefects, although Voldemort was Head Boy while Hermione skipped school during what would have been her seventh year due to political persecution, preventing her from being Head Girl that year (it is possible that Hermione became Head Girl when she went back to finish her seventh year after Voldemort's final destruction). They both came from Muggle backgrounds, but Voldemort was raised in an orphanage while Hermione was brought up in a loving Muggle family.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=56" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You're lying, filthy mud-blood, and I know it! You have been inside my vault in Gringotts! Tell the truth, tell the truth! What else did you take? What else have you got? Tell me the truth or, I swear, I shall run you through with this knife! What else did you take, what else? ANSWER ME! </i>CRUCIO<i>!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Bellatrix interrogating Hermione<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 166px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="164" height="228" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" decoding="async" width="164" height="228" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, a hated enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix Lestrange was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s most fanatically loyal followers; Hermione initially knew her as one of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> involved in torturing and permanently incapacitating <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice Longbottom</a>, though she also witnessed Bellatrix murder <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>, Bellatrix chose to torture Hermione, who, as a Muggle-born, Bellatrix felt was most dispensable (though, as a "<i>blood traitor,</i>" Ron Weasley was a close second), in order to discover where and how the trio had managed to acquire <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a>. During the interrogation, Bellatrix used her knife to carve the word "<i>mudblood</i>" on Hermione's arm,<sup id="cite_ref-DHF1_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHF1-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> as well as torturing her sadistically with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Hermione later used one of Bellatrix's hairs obtained in the skirmish to make <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> and <a href="/wiki/Break-in_of_Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank_(1998)" title="Break-in of Gringotts Wizarding Bank (1998)">break into</a> the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Vault" title="Lestrange Vault">Lestrange Vault</a> at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a>. She expressed disgust at having to  use Bellatrix's wand knowing the crimes Bellatrix commited with it. Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a> duelled against Bellatrix during the final battle, but were made to stand aside by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>, who eventually killed Bellatrix herself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Draco_Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=57" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Don’t you dare call Hagrid pathetic, you foul — you evil —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Hermione!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Get off, Ron!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione after slapping Draco for mocking a distraught Hagrid<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="243" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140623200347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140623200347" decoding="async" width="160" height="243" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140623200347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, her school bully</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Draco Malfoy, of an old and wealthy <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">family</a> with <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> ties, was raised to believe in the inferiority of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, and thus treated Hermione with disdain. This was probably exacerbated by Hermione's friendship with Harry and Ron, who shared a strong enmity with Draco from virtually the moment they met, and her beating Draco in school marks, for which his <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">father</a> berated him.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Draco frequently called Hermione the disparaging term "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>," which usually set off the tempers of her friends — and the entire <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_team" title="Quidditch team">Quidditch team</a> when he first said it to her face in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a><sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> — but Hermione tended to ignore Draco and urged Harry and Ron to do the same. 
</p><p>Occasionally she would snap back at him, and in their third year, she even slapped him when he mocked <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> for being upset over the impending execution of <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>, for which Draco was largely responsible.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In spite of his prejudice and dislike toward Hermione, Draco was reluctant to confirm her identity when he was asked to do so by his parents and aunt <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, avoiding even looking at her. As an adult sobered by his wartime experiences, Draco was civil towards Hermione and her friends, and friendly with her nephew, Albus Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>He even found the idea of taking orders from her during their ambush in 1981 of Delphini to be darkly humorous. Draco's civility towards Hermione during this time was likely reinforced due to her being the Minister For Magic in Britain at the time, and possibly due to her relations to Albus Potter, the best friend of his own son, Scorpius. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pansy_Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=58" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Pansy Parkinson">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Pansy Parkinson"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Stunningly pretty? </i>Her<i>? What was she judging against — a chipmunk?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Pansy about Hermione when her looks are complimented in an article<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20141024191624" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="218" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pansy Parkinson infobox.png" data-image-key="Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141024191624" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20141024191624" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141024191624" decoding="async" width="165" height="218" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pansy Parkinson infobox.png" data-image-key="Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141024191624" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pansy_Parkinson_infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pansy Parkinson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> was more or less Hermione's polar opposite: where Hermione was compassionate (as seen when she founded <a href="/wiki/Society_for_the_Promotion_of_Elfish_Welfare" title="Society for the Promotion of Elfish Welfare">SPEW</a>), independent, and incredibly helpful to nearly anyone who needed it, Pansy was petty and spiteful, who mocked just about every non-Slytherin student she encountered (as well as <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>), and was little more than one of Draco Malfoy's more sycophantic <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s gang">lackeys</a>. Pansy had a tendency to taunt and snipe at Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> at any given opportunity, though Hermione rarely seemed more than slightly irritated by her comments; the major exception to that most likely would have been Pansy's attempt to surrender Harry to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> shortly prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Hermione had a scathing opinion of Pansy, believing her to be be a "cow", and "thicker than a concussed troll".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rita_Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=59" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rita Skeeter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Rita Skeeter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>I </i>hate<i> that Skeeter woman! I'll get her back for this if it's the last thing I do!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione vows retribution against Rita Skeeter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101113194128" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="221" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rita Skeeter 2.jpg" data-image-key="Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101113194128" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101113194128" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101113194128" decoding="async" width="166" height="221" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rita Skeeter 2.jpg" data-image-key="Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/23/Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20101113194128" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rita_Skeeter_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While covering the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> in Hermione's fourth year, <a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a> journalist <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> wrote a number of exaggerated and slanderous stories about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and his friends, including one that outed <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>. Harry and Hermione angrily confronted Rita about this. After Hermione insulted her, Rita published another article that portrayed Hermione as manipulative and ambitious, claiming that she was toying with the emotions of both Harry Potter and <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>. This resulted in Hermione receiving several letters of hate mail, including a few <a href="/wiki/Howler" title="Howler">Howlers</a> and at least one envelope filled with <a href="/wiki/Bubotuber_pus" title="Bubotuber pus">bubotuber pus</a>.
</p><p>Hermione became obsessed with getting back at Rita and uncovering how she was getting all of her information. Finally, near the end of the school year Hermione realised that Rita Skeeter was an unregistered <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>. She caught Rita in her beetle form attempting to eavesdrop on Harry in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Third Task</a>. Hermione sealed her inside a small bottle. Hermione blackmailed Rita into giving up writing for one year, otherwise her unregistered status would be revealed. As the penalties are apparently quite severe, Rita had no choice but to comply.
</p><p>When the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> began using the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> in its smear campaign against Harry, Hermione was again able to blackmail Rita, this time into writing an article for <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i> that would allow Harry to tell his side of the story. After her one year punishment was over, Rita went back to writing with as much enthusiasm and as little scruples as she had before, although it's unknown if she ever crossed Hermione again. Given her notable lack of commentary regarding Hermione during the 2014 Quidditch World Cup in Egypt, it is likely that Rita remained extremely wary of Hermione's wrath 19 years following her being blackmailed by the prodigious witch.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Organisations">Organisations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=60" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Organisations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Organisations"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=61" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>I also think we should have a name... It would promote a feeling of team spirit and unity, don't you think?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione on naming the Army<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, her allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's Army was essentially Hermione's brainchild, though she co-founded it with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>. After <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> informed her <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> students that they would not be using any magic, claiming a theoretical education would suffice, a furious Hermione (fearful of being ill-equipped to deal with the reborn <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>) conceived of the organisation as a means of allowing any student interested in actually practising defensive magic to do so. Though the secret classes were taught by Harry, Hermione arranged the initial meeting at the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>, created the DA's method of covert <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_coin" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army coin">communication</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">jinxed</a> their member list to reveal any betrayal. 
</p><p>All of the DA members grew closer over the course of the year (with the exceptions of <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>, who betrayed the DA to Umbridge, and later <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, who deserted them), as evidenced by their reunion in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, and their enthusiasm in supporting Harry and mobilising against the invading Death Eaters during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Moreover, the DA truly cemented Hermione's friendships with <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, who were the only members, aside from <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, to fight alongside Hermione, Harry, and Ron at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=62" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>So what is this place?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Headquarters.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Of the Order of the Phoenix. It's a secret society. Dumbledore formed it back when they first fought You-Know-Who.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione explaining to Harry the Order<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div> 
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150206155602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, her allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione first heard about the Order of the Phoenix in 1995, when she, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> spent several weeks at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">the Order's headquarters</a>. Through her time at Grimmauld Place, Hermione got to know <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, the most famous <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> of modern times, known for rounding up several <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> after the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> and for his growing paranoia. He and Hermione fought together in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, and later, in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, where Moody was killed by Voldemort's own hand. Hermione, like the rest of the Order, was shocked and horrified by the death of such a skilled Auror, "<i>the consummate survivor</i>,"<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and disgusted by <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>'s desertion. Hermione, who had known Fletcher as a petty criminal who had stolen a number the Black family heirlooms shortly after <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>'s death, aside from being a member of the Order, took part in interrogating Fletcher, when she, Harry and Ron realised <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> had been among the items stolen from Grimmauld Place.
</p><p>Hermione had great respect for <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, a skilled Auror and eventual <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>, who was known as "Royal" on <i><a href="/wiki/Potterwatch" title="Potterwatch">Potterwatch</a></i>, and who saved countless lives (including Hermione, Ron and Harry's) when he sent his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to warn the attendees of <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">Bill and Fleur's wedding</a> that the Ministry had fallen, and with it, the protections surrounding <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a>. Another member of the Order responsible for saving the trio was <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, Albus' younger brother. Though Hermione, Harry and Ron had known him for some time as the owner of the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head Pub</a>, they finally met him in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, just before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, when he just barely managed to get them out a trap set by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Prior to that, he sent Dobby to rescue them, along with <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> and <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a> the Goblin, from the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>; as it turned out, Aberforth had acquired Sirius Black's <a href="/wiki/Two-way_mirror" title="Two-way mirror">two-way mirror</a> from Mundungus Fletcher, and been keeping an eye out for Harry.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, a funny, <a href="/wiki/Metamorphmagus" title="Metamorphmagus">Metamorphmagus</a> witch, who had become a good friend of Hermione's, died along with her husband and fellow member of the Order, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. As their son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Ted Lupin</a>, was Harry's godson and was also dating Hermione's niece, <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire</a> by 2017, it's likely Hermione remained quite close to him.
</p>
<h3><span id="Professors_&amp;_Other_Hogwarts_Staff"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Professors_.26_Other_Hogwarts_Staff">Professors &amp; Other Hogwarts Staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=63" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Professors &amp; Other Hogwarts Staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Professors &amp; Other Hogwarts Staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=64" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Second — to Miss Hermione Granger... for the use of cool logic in the face of fire, I award Gryffindor house fifty points!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dumbledore awarding Hermione last-minute points at the feast at the end of her first year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, her former headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As with most aspects of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>, Hermione read about <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> shortly after learning that she was a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>. Hermione on her very first train journey revealed she wanted to be in Gryffindor because it was the house that Dumbledore belonged to. She first met the Hogwarts headmaster during her her first year at the school, in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, and quickly came to respect Dumbledore's immense power and seemingly infinite wisdom. Although Dumbledore was not as close with her as he was with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, he showed great insight into her character very early on. She was one of only three students Dumbledore bequeathed a personal item, as he believed her to be, along with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, trustworthy of accompanying Harry on his mission to destroy <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>.
</p><p>He respected her intellect, perspicacity, and level-headedness, admitting to Harry that he had counted on Hermione to keep things in perspective when the trio finally discovered the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>. Hermione was devastated when Dumbledore was killed, and visited his <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait">portrait</a> with Harry and Ron after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> to determine the fate of the Hallows.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rubeus_Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=65" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Then I'll go back again tomorrow. I'll plan his lessons for him if I have to. I don't care if <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">she</a> throws out <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Trelawney</a> but she's not getting rid of Hagrid.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione defending Hagrid against Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" decoding="async" width="165" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20160121163026" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, her friend and professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Rubeus Hagrid was the <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">Gamekeeper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> professor at Hogwarts, as well as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First</a> and <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding Wars</a>. Since Hagrid had met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> prior to the start of Hermione's first year at Hogwarts, Hermione grew closer to Hagrid as her friendship with Harry developed, eventually coming to visit him in his <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid%27s_cabin" class="mw-redirect" title="Rubeus Hagrid&#39;s cabin">hut</a> regularly with Harry and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>. In their second year, Hagrid comforted Hermione when she was called a "<i>a filthy little mudblood</i>" by Draco Malfoy. 
</p><p>Though she disapproved of Hagrid's penchant for collecting dangerous <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">pets</a>, she tended to more pro-actively support him in his efforts to care for them than Harry and Ron, as when Hagrid was attempting to appeal the execution of <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> and raise his half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a>. In turn, it was Hagrid who encouraged Ron and Harry to re-think their treatment of Hermione when the three had a brief falling out over Hermione getting Harry's new <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> confiscated in their third year. When <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> threatened Hagrid's job during the 1995-1996 school year, Hermione advised him to teach only materials related to their O.W.Ls, so as not to give Umbridge any excuse to fire him, and worked tirelessly to keep him on track.
</p><p>Hagrid remained close to the trio throughout their time at Hogwarts, and fought various battles in the course of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. In <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Harry's sons planned to meet Hagrid in his hut for tea soon after arriving at school, and it's very likely that Hermione and Ron's <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">daughter</a> would have been joining them.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Remus_Lupin">Remus Lupin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=66" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione</b>: "<i>Harry! How could you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>You shouldn't have said that stuff to Lupin.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron, after Harry yells at Remus for leaving his wife<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119235913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119235913" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20161119235913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, her professor and friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was among the students who were very impressed by Remus Lupin's teaching in 1993, when he was appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor. Hermione deduced he was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> during the school year, yet chose to keep it a secret in order to respect his privacy. Towards the end of the year, however, Lupin admitted that he was a werewolf to Harry, Ron and Hermione whilst in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. Following the events in this dilapidated building, Lupin became fully prepared to help <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> kill <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, the wizard who betrayed <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>. 
</p><p>However, thanks to Harry's intervention, they chose not to commit the murder, inadvertently allowing Pettigrew to escape. Lupin had referred to Hermione as the cleverest witch of her age he had ever seen before to this. Hermione, meanwhile, did not concern herself with Lupin's lycanthropy, she judged him only by his good nature and the content of his character.
</p><p>Hermione met Lupin again in 1995 at the <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">Headquarters</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. She and Lupin both fought against the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> in 1996, and survived (despite Hermione being side-swiped by Dolohov's curse). They also fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> alongside, both emerging alive and relatively unscathed on the two occasions. Hermione was pleased to learn that Lupin had married <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a> before the Battle of the Seven Potters began, and became even more joyful at the news of Lupin's son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Ted Lupin</a>, being born; joining in on the celebratory festivities at <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>. Hermione was devastated by Lupin's and Tonks' <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">deaths</a> in 1998, becoming friendly with their orphaned son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a>, later on in life.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=67" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Professor McGonagall</b>: "<i>Potter! Weasley! What are you doing?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Hermione. We haven't seen her for ages, Professor, and we thought we'd sneak into the hospital wing, you know, and tell her the Mandrakes are nearly ready and, er, not to worry.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Professor McGonagall</b>: "<i>Of course. Of course, I realise this has all been hardest on the friends of those who have been… I quite understand. Yes, Potter, of course you may visit Miss Granger, I will inform Professor Binns where you've gone. Tell Madam Pomfrey I have given you permission.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Professor Minerva McGonagall softening when Harry and Ron tell her they want to visit Hermione<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="227" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20150810172040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20150810172040" decoding="async" width="160" height="227" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20150810172040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, her Head of House and professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Professor Minerva McGonagall took a shine to Hermione from the first class she had with her, granting the first-year student in <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">her house</a> one of her "<i>rare smiles</i>" when Hermione successfully <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">transfigured</a> a match into a needle early on in the lesson and long before any other student. She had high expectations for Hermione, and was thus disappointed in her when Hermione claimed she tried to fight the <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">troll</a> that entered the school in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> on her own, in order to cover up for Harry and Ron. Whenever Hermione and her friends would get into trouble, McGonagall almost inevitably looked to Hermione to be the most sensible one.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_3-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>McGonagall was noticeably upset when Hermione was <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, even granting Harry and Ron permission to skip a class so they could visit Hermione in the hospital wing.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_21-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/1993%E2%80%931994_school_year" title="1993–1994 school year">following school year</a>, she helped arrange for Hermione to be granted a <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">Time-Turner</a> to take extra classes.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> When the professor was injured with four <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spells</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Hermione was very upset and worried for her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_20-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Hermione seemed to regard her head of house as a role model, while Professor McGonagall, in spite of her sternness, was obviously quite fond of Hermione and expected great things of her.
</p><p>Later, after McGonagall became headmistress of Hogwarts and Hermione became a member of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, McGonagall granted her permission to use notes left to the Hogwarts Archives, written by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, in her re-translation of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tales_of_Beedle_the_Bard" title="The Tales of Beedle the Bard">The Tales of Beedle the Bard </a></i>, demonstrating McGonagall's trust in her former pupil.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=68" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Please, sir, the <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> differs from the true <a href="/wiki/Wolf" title="Wolf">wolf</a> in several small ways.The snout of the werewolf —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>That is the second time you have spoken out of turn, Miss Granger, Five more points from Gryffindor for being an insufferable know-it-all.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape insulting Hermione<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 157px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150307193047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="155" height="231" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20150307193047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150307193047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20150307193047" decoding="async" width="155" height="231" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a3/Severus_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/155?cb=20150307193047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, her professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape was the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Master</a> during most of Hermione's time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. He was also the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a>, and tended to openly show preferential treatment for the students of his own house, while being quick to criticise and deduct points from <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students. He was particularly unpleasant towards the trio, and regularly punished and verbally assaulted Harry and Ron for their poor to mediocre performances in his class. He could not do the same to Hermione, as she was the best student in the year and instead mocked her for things like being an "<i>insufferable know-it-all,</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-POA_15-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> once even snidely insulting the size of Hermione's teeth.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_22-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his pre-existing dislike for Gryffindor,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_7-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Snape's treatment of Hermione likely had more to do with her close friendship with Harry. Despite this, Hermione was still seen to defend Snape on occasion when Harry and Ron blamed him for evil deeds which occurred in <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, like setting the troll in the dungeon and trying to steal the Philosopher's Stone in Harry's first year. In her fifth year she defended Snape while Ron expressed distrust of him, citing the number of times they were wrong about Snape wanting to harm them. After Dumbledore's death, she like many, believed that Snape was a coward who killed a man who trusted him more than anyone. It is unknown exactly how she reacted to learning of Snape's true motives and allegiance, but given her personality, it is highly likely that she came to both forgive her former Professor's cruelty, and even admire him for his bravery.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dolores_Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=69" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>That foul, evil old gargoyle! We're not learn how to defend ourselves, we're not learning how to pass our O.W.L.s... she's taking over the entire school!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione's outrage on Umbridge's take-over of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Dolores_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101120104908" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Dolores_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101120104908" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Dolores_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101120104908" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Dolores_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101120104908" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/94/Dolores_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20101120104908" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, her former professor and enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dolores Umbridge was appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. She was a sadistic woman who enjoyed punishing and torturing students using the <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a>, most notably when she forced <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to carve <i>"I must not tell lies</i>" into the back of his own hand. Umbridge was as obsessed with blood-status as the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, and had a particular hatred of what she called "<i>half-breeds</i>." Hermione, like most of the students and staff at Hogwarts, hated Umbridge. Hermione was one of the first to pick up on the true motives behind Umbridge's appointment at the magical school. In turn, Umbridge was not too fond of Hermione, who was not only <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a>, but was also probably far too perceptive for her liking, as well as being outspokenly opposed to a purely theoretical <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">defensive</a> magical education. 
</p><p>When Umbridge planned to use <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> and then the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on Harry, Hermione was the one who came up with the lie that led to them venturing into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and Umbridge eventually being dragged away by a <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">herd of offended centaurs</a>.
</p><p>Hermione next met Umbridge a second time at the Ministry of Magic in 1997, when Hermione was disguised as <a href="/wiki/Mafalda_Hopkirk" title="Mafalda Hopkirk">Mafalda Hopkirk</a> through the usage of <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>. Umbridge was, at the time, interrogating "Mudblood" witches and wizards, prior to sending them to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. Harry stunned Umbridge and retrieved <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a>, one of Voldemort's hocruxes which Umbridge had taken from <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a> and was attempting to pass off as a family heirloom and proof of her relation to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>. Hermione replaced the locket by duplicating it with the Geminio spell so Umbridge would not know that it had been taken from her. The trio proceeded to free all the Muggle-Borns awaiting interrogation.
</p><p>Suffice it to say that Umbridge personified everything that Hermione detested and loathed in Wizarding society, including but not limited to racial prejudice, sadism, malicious misuse of power, authoritarianism, and pure-blood supremacy. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Septima_Vector">Septima Vector</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=70" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Septima Vector">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Septima Vector"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hermione also had a good relationship with her <a href="/wiki/Arithmancy" title="Arithmancy">Arithmancy</a> <a href="/wiki/Septima_Vector" title="Septima Vector">Professor Septima Vector</a>. Many students disliked Vector because of her strictness. However, Hermione said Arithmancy was her favourite subject at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She also never complained about Vector's strictness. During her <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third year</a>, Hermione joined her class and used a <a href="/wiki/Time-turner" class="mw-redirect" title="Time-turner">time-turner</a> to get to one of the lessons.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Then in her <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a>, Hermione and the other students got no homework from Septima Vector on the first day of term,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> and she adamantly refused to skive Arithmancy.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?veaction=edit&amp;section=71" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger?action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Rowling took Hermione's name from William Shakespeare's <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Winter%27s_Tale" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Winter&#39;s Tale">The Winter's Tale</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-TNPC1999_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TNPC1999-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> saying that she wanted it to be unusual, since if fewer girls shared her name, fewer girls would get teased for it.<sup id="cite_ref-TNPC1999_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TNPC1999-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Rowling's knowledge and interest in Greek mythology may have also influenced her choice in regards to Hermione's name. In 1988, Rowling wrote a short essay about her time studying classics entitled <i>"What was the Name of that Nymph Again? or Greek and Roman Studies Recalled";</i> it was published by the University of Exeter's journal <i>Pegasus</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> The name "Hermione" is derived from "Hermes", who was the messenger of the Greek gods, as well as the god of wit, eloquence and quick thinking.
</p><p>
‘Hermione’ is the female derivative of ‘Hermes’, a messenger god known for his sharp wit and ability to transition between worlds. Quite fittingly, Hermione transitioned between the Muggle and wizarding worlds, delivered information, and was pretty sharp-witted herself.</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Her1265.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100709172531" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Her1265.jpg" data-image-key="Her1265.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Her1265.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100709172531" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Her1265.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100709172531" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Her1265.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100709172531" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Her1265.jpg" data-image-key="Her1265.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Her1265.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100709172531" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Her1265.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione in her <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">sixth year</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hermione_(mythology)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hermione (mythology)">Hermione</a> is also the name of another figure from Greek mythology, who was the princess of Sparta and the only daughter of Helen of Troy and King Menelaus. The name also appears in Jean-Baptiste Lully's play <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cadmus_et_Hermione" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cadmus et Hermione">Cadmus et Hermione</a></i>, based on the story of the goddess of harmony, Harmonia, who married the founder of Thebes. 
</p><p>In order to ensure that fans could correctly pronounce Hermione's name, a scene was created between Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i> in which they discuss the correct pronunciation; however, the closest Krum got was "Herm-own-ninny."<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Will_and_Testament_of_Albus_Percival_Wulfric_Brian_Dumbledore" title="The Last Will and Testament of Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore">will</a> of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, Hermione's middle name was listed as "Jean;" however, in previous interviews, Rowling had stated that her middle name was "Jane."
